Wang Yongbin Discusses Judicial Affairs in Five Provinces 34

(Nanjing) Wang Yongbin recently completed an inspection of judicial affairs in various provinces, including Hubei, Hunan, Guangdong, Jiangxi, and Anhui. He returned to Beijing from Wuhu on the 20th, and senior officials of the Ministry of Justice welcomed him. After entering the city, Wang immediately returned to the Ministry of Justice to rest. When reporters inquired about the inspection, Wang said that judicial affairs in the provinces have made significant progress. Since the central government reorganized judicial affairs in Guangdong Province, it has strictly ordered the unification of laws and regulations, rectified official discipline, and created a new atmosphere. It has also implemented a three-level, three-trial system. Although the reorganization period has been short, the results are already visible. Judicial officials in Hubei, Hunan, Jiangxi, and Anhui provinces are generally able to implement laws and regulations and work hard to clear backlogged cases. New prisons are also under construction in each province. Since the implementation of the Provisional Regulations for the Simplification of Prison Procedures, the number of ordinary criminal offenders has been greatly reduced. However, the number of prisoners detained by military agencies is still too high, and prisons are still crowded. It is still necessary to consult with military agencies to resolve this issue. Every time I go to a province, I urge the active establishment of county judicial offices as a foundation for the future widespread establishment of local courts. According to the current situation, this plan can be implemented, because county magistrates in various provinces hope to establish local courts as soon as possible so that they can concentrate on political affairs. After the reorganization of county court revenues by the Ministry of Justice, there has been an increase, and the goal of self-sufficiency is not far off. This proves that breaking the entrenched habit of not separating administrative and judicial powers is not difficult. Based on the observations made during this trip, it is my opinion that we have previously focused too much on higher-level judicial agencies and neglected to rectify lower-level judicial agencies, which is a mistake. Because the first-level courts and county prisons are most closely related to the interests of the people, and their facilities are the least perfect, the people feel extremely painful. In the future, the Ministry will devote all its efforts to rectifying the first-level courts and county prisons. He also discussed the issue of establishing a special district court in Kowloon, saying that the situation in Kowloon is different from that in Hong Kong. Kowloon is only a leased territory and has not been ceded. However, the people there often appeal to the Hong Kong court, which is detrimental to sovereignty. Therefore, I went to inspect the area and consulted with Diao Zuqian to establish a court in accordance with the precedent of the Shanghai Special District Court to handle appeals from the local people. In the future, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Justice will jointly carry out this work. (Central News Agency dispatch, 20th)

The Rural Areas of Changshu (Part 1) 42

— Jin Yong

Blessed Land of Yushan

If you have been to Changshu, you will surely see a large wooden plaque at the foot of Yushan Mountain with the four characters "虞山福地" (Yushan Blessed Land) written on it.

Changshu is a prosperous area in Jiangsu Province, indeed worthy of the two words "blessed land." Weng Tonghe of the Qing Dynasty was from Changshu, so at that time there were eight satires on Li Hongzhang and Weng Tonghe, making a couplet saying: "The Prime Minister of Hefei makes the world thin, and the Minister of Agriculture Changshu makes the world desolate." Although the desolation of the world is not because of Changshu's constant good harvests, it is certainly true that Changshu is a good place.

Changshu County is located in the center of four townships, with Yushan Mountain to the northwest. Part of the mountain area extends into the city, so the ancients had the famous line "Ten li of green mountains, half entering the city."

Yushan Mountain is not very large. If you are a brisk walker, one day is enough for you to explore its depths and discover its beauty. In Changshu, you will feel what mountain spirituality and water beauty are all about. If you don't believe it, you can stand on the road to Jianmen (the most magnificent place in Yushan, with steep cliffs and a small path), and look out. You will see clear blue lake water, lush misty trees, and squares of fields planted with very orderly and vibrant crops, a yellow patch, a green patch, and a blue patch. Seeing this will not only make you feel refreshed, but it will also make you want to crush these crops, mash them up, and eat them with the fertile mud. You will say, "It is truly a 'Yushan Blessed Land'!"

Three Types of Bloodsuckers in the Countryside

In Changshu, there are three types of people who suck the blood and flesh of farmers. Relying on their inherent or newly acquired power, they parasitize this blessed land and harm the farmers, ruthlessly swallowing up the fertile land and yellow, green, and blue crops that the farmers own.

Changshu is famous for producing rice, but the areas that exclusively grow rice are limited to the southeast townships because the rivers and ports are wide and the land is fertile, truly worthy of being called a land of fish and rice. As for the northwest townships, half of them grow rice and half grow cotton. The rice is only enough for self-sufficiency, and most of the cotton is sold. Only the sandbar area, all of which is sandy land silted up from the Yangtze River, is planted with cotton nine-tenths of the time and rice one-tenth of the time, forming another crop area.

However, the prosperous farmland is not owned by the farmers, and the abundant products are not possessed by the farmers. The farmers work hard all year round, but what they gain is exploited layer upon layer by people who do not work.

In Changshu, farmland is concentrated in the hands of landlords. In my estimation, less than four-tenths of the farmers are self-cultivating. There are even fewer self-cultivating farmers in the southeast townships. Originally, landlords own many fields and can easily exploit the farmers, but the general landlords of Changshu have an additional layer of power and take on another form, which is that they mostly possess a kind of political power. Many of the large landlords have served as officials, so the bigger the official, the more land they have; the more land one has, the easier it is to become an official.

Large landlords often employ many rent collectors and accountants, who directly exercise power and exploit the farmers. The farmers cannot calculate and have no choice but to let them profit from it. When farmers pay rent with rice, they must put a few more liters in each bag, because the landlord's measures are comparatively larger.

The government serves them. Every autumn and winter, one can see the yamen runners running around in the four townships, and groups of poor farmers following them to the city, either pawning things to pay rent or facing lawsuits.

The second type of bloodsucker is the tax collector. Not only do they directly extort an extra one or two cents from the farmers' taxes, but it is said that the greatest gain is still from exploiting those who have land without proof or grain without roots.

After the land survey, this chronic problem may be eliminated, but tens of thousands of (estimated by some to be around 100,000) coins every year are the blood and sweat of the farmers, yet they have been eaten by them for generations.

The third type of bloodsucker seems to be a specialty of the counties along the river because there are often silted sandy lands along the Yangtze River that can be reclaimed. Before the reclamation, there are a group of people called "sand bullies" who report to the county that they have thousands or tens of thousands of acres of sandy land in a certain place and are willing to pay a few cents per acre so that the sand bullies can enjoy the benefits as the sandy land slowly accumulates. In order to not spend too much money and reap great profits, the sand bullies compete very fiercely. Whenever a piece of sandy land is to be enclosed, it is necessary to gather hundreds or thousands of hardworking farmers to compete with each other to enclose the sandy land. The side with the greater power will enclose more land. As a result, there are often armed fights, and injuries and deaths are common.

After the sand bullies use the farmers to enclose the sandy land, they either sell it to the farmers, making a profit of fifty or sixty yuan on a capital of only ten yuan. The farmers do not get any benefit at all. Or they rent it to the farmers to cultivate. Because the area is close to the river, it is prone to floods and typhoons, so when the sand bullies rent the land to the farmers, they first require the farmers to pay the so-called "board rent." In the event of crop failures, the farmers are fully responsible. The farmers create them into rich people, and they immediately come to absorb the remaining blood in their veins.

The Future of World Silver Prices 43

— Fortunately

Since the United States began large-scale purchases of silver in 1933, world silver prices have gradually risen. By May 1935, due to the American monopoly in the world silver market, silver prices began to plummet. It was not until mid-January of this year that they stabilized. From that time until the beginning of this month, silver prices in New York did not fluctuate greatly. In the history of the world silver market, this can be considered the longest period of silver price stability. However, recently, world silver prices have changed again. From November 6th, silver prices in London and Mumbai suddenly rose sharply. From the 9th, the price of foreign silver in New York followed suit. In the past few days, silver prices in various places seem to have slightly declined, but they have not yet fallen to the level of silver prices during the stable period before this month.

To understand why silver prices have suddenly risen this time, one must first recognize that the United States occupies a dominant position in the current world silver market. This can be proven with statistics. In 1934, the total world silver production reached 180 million ounces. The total exports of silver-using countries reached 260 million ounces, totaling 440 million ounces. Among them, the U.S. government purchased 310 million ounces. In 1935, it purchased even more, not only swallowing up the world's total silver production of 210 million ounces and speculators' stockpiles of 160 million ounces, but also absorbing a large portion of the exports of silver-using countries, totaling more than 540 million ounces. For the current year up to the end of September, according to a report from the U.S. Department of Commerce, the silver absorbed by the United States was worth a huge 150 million U.S. dollars. At 45 cents per ounce, the amount of silver totaled 330 million ounces. This is already much more than the amount absorbed in the entire year of 1934.

Since the United States is currently the only largest customer in the world for silver, speculators in free silver markets no longer seem to have the possibility of manipulating silver prices. We can clearly see that the current silver price is merely a market price set by the U.S. government for individual countries, and it differs in nature from the market price of a free silver market. World silver can no longer be regarded as an ordinary commodity.

This kind of silver market phenomenon not only makes it impossible for world silver speculators to operate, but more importantly, it makes those countries that use silver as a reserve for international payments feel considerable hidden anxieties. Although China has now broken away from the silver standard, it still uses silver as a currency reserve. Under the current circumstances, only if we can find appropriate adjustment methods in international payments, and only if we can live without "capital exports," will our currency value not be seriously affected by changes in silver prices.

Mining Poison Sedimentation Pond Breaks at the Summit of Mount Osarizawa, Japan; More Than a Thousand Nearby Residents Buried Alive; Many Corpses Float Away with Toxic Mud 44

(Tokyo) Regarding the tragic accident of the collapse of the Osarizawa mining poison sedimentation pond, according to a telegram from the Akita Prefectural Governor to the Minister of Home Affairs on the 20th, the number of households affected has reached more than 300. The number of bodies discovered so far is 54. However, there are still those floating away, and others buried at the same time as their houses, numbering over 300. In the future, when excavating corpses, it may be necessary to request military assistance. The number of households affected is 300, with an average of 5 family members per household, the number of victims reaches 1,500. Currently, only 75 people have been confirmed to be alive. The others are unknown. Furthermore, the bodies of the victims are under highly toxic mud, so excavation will still take two or three days. (20th, Domei News Agency)

Osarizawa: Mr. Osato, the director of the Hanawa-cho Hospital, said to reporters at the scene of the accident that the number of deaths seems to exceed 1,000. Underneath this mud, there are still hundreds of dead bodies. Because the reservoir contains mining poison, many victims drank the water, making it difficult to sustain life. (20th, same dispatch)

Osarizawa: After the collapse of the mining poison sedimentation pond, the six villages outside Osarizawa have become a tragic toxic mud street, completely submerged by red-black toxic mud, with an extremely foul odor, creating a desolate scene that is heartbreaking. Three hundred households are buried under six to twenty feet of sulfurized mud, resulting in the sacrifice of over a thousand people. Fathers search for their sons, wives seek their husbands, their cries of grief are unbearable to hear. Entering the green toxic mud is like taking poison, making it difficult to preserve life. Contact with the skin causes immediate corrosion. Its toxicity is evident. Currently, rescuers from various places are arriving successively to provide assistance, and excavation teams are also tearfully excavating, searching for bodies. (20th, Domei News Agency)

Akita: The embankment of Nakanosawa, at the summit of the Osarizawa Mine in Kazuno County, Akita Prefecture, suddenly collapsed at around 4:00 this morning. Over one hundred houses of the mine company's employees and workers below were swept into the Yoneshiro River by the muddy torrent, creating a living hell. After the accident, the fire brigade rang bells to summon members and the self-defense force to engage in rescue work. Because houses swept away blocked the flow of the Yoneshiro River, causing it to overflow, the surrounding area became a swamp. Rescue teams saved only a dozen or so people, with hundreds more unable to be helped. (20th, Domei News Agency)

Hanawa: After the collapse of the reservoir at the Osarizawa Mine, 136 houses in Uribata Village, 80 houses in Sasagoya, 50 houses in Shinhotta, and 70 houses in other places in the downstream area, totaling 336 households, were all swept away by the flood. Of the 1,300 residents, only 18 were rescued. 22 bodies have been discovered, with the rest missing. Their survival is almost hopeless. After the floodwaters passed, only a few houses remained in the affected villages, and the surrounding area has become a sea of mud. Houses and furniture are floating on the surface of the Yoneshiro River, and bodies are found everywhere, a very tragic sight. (20th, Domei News Agency)

Hanawa: The tragic accident of the collapse of the reservoir at the Osarizawa Mine occurred before dawn, making rescue completely impossible. More than a thousand nearby residents were buried alive in the mud and water. By 10:30 this morning, over 300 bodies had been discovered upstream of the Yoneshiro River. After receiving the report, the Akita Prefectural Police Department mobilized all police officers, and the police stations in Kazuno and Kitaakita also dispatched police officers and firefighters to engage in rescue efforts. The Akita branch hospital of the Red Cross Society and officials from the prefectural health department have also dispatched numerous doctors and nurses to provide assistance. (20th, Domei News Agency)

French Aviator Crashes Near Nagasaki; Plane Hits Mountain Peak and Shatters Upon Impact; Mr. Chappy Seriously Injured, Achievement Falls Short 45

(Tokyo) French aviator Mr. Chappy took off from Hong Kong at 5:25 yesterday morning, completing the final stage of his long-distance flight between Paris and Tokyo. Unexpectedly, news arrived that Mr. Chappy's plane had crashed and shattered 65 miles from Nagasaki. Mr. Chappy suffered a head injury and a broken leg. Although the situation is quite serious, hope for survival remains. Mr. Chappy's flight was intended to win the 400,000 franc prize offered by the aviation department for a long-distance flight between Paris and Tokyo. Since departing from Paris, the journey had been extremely smooth. After taking off from Hong Kong yesterday morning and arriving northwest of Nagasaki, the aircraft suddenly encountered an obstacle and was forced to land. The area happened to be a mountain 1,000 meters high. The plane crashed into the mountain peak and shattered completely. The time was 4:30 yesterday afternoon, but no one noticed at the time. It was not until four hours later that a charcoal burner found it. He carried Mr. Chappy to the foot of the mountain and administered emergency treatment. It is said that Mr. Chappy was unconscious when he was rescued. Many people had already gathered at the Tokyo airfield to welcome Mr. Chappy. When the plane was overdue, they knew that something must have happened en route. The initial news of Mr. Chappy's accident was transmitted from the police station to Moji at 1:40 this morning and immediately relayed to Tokyo. The charcoal burner who rescued Mr. Chappy heard a loud noise when the plane crashed, but couldn't find it until four hours later, as the mountain forest was very dense and searching was extremely difficult. (20th, Reuters)

Moji: Mr. Chappy set out from Paris and flew 15,000 kilometers. It is a pity that his grand plan failed at the last step. His flight time for the 14,000 kilometers was 78 hours, which is an astonishing record. (20th, Domei News Agency)

(Paris) News of Mr. Chappy's injury reached Paris on the night of the 19th, causing national shock due to the unexpected event. Although Mr. Chappy was unable to win the 300,000 franc prize, the French government has recognized Mr. Chappy's bravery and achievements. Therefore, it was decided on the night of the 19th to award Mr. Chappy the Fourth Class Medal as a reward for his efforts. (20th, Domei News Agency)

Fukuoka: Since French aviator Mr. Chappy departed from Hong Kong at 5:25 yesterday morning, news has been scarce. However, at around 8:00 p.m. on the 19th, villagers from Sefuri Village, Kanzaki County, Saga Prefecture, Japan, discovered the plane crashed in the Sefuri Mountains. The aircraft body was severely damaged. They immediately notified the police station. Police Inspector Yoshida led doctors and interpreters to provide immediate rescue. It is said that the plane crashed in the mountains at around 3:00 p.m. on the 19th. Mr. Chappy suffered injuries to his head and thigh, but they are not life-threatening. (20th, Domei News Agency)

Sefuri Village: Kuboyama in Sefuri Village, where Mr. Chappy's plane crashed, is crowded with prefectural hall staff, military police, police officers, and newspaper reporters arriving by car. Villagers, regardless of age or gender, are all comforting and caring for Mr. Chappy and discussing the circumstances of Mr. Chappy's accident. Therefore, Mr. Chappy's ability to preserve his life can be called a miracle. If it had been delayed by two hours, he might have lost his life due to excessive bleeding or intolerance to the severe cold. Furthermore, Mr. Chappy's condition is improving well, so he will be transferred to the prefectural hospital or Kyushu Imperial University Hospital for treatment within a day or two. (20th, Domei News Agency)

Mount Sefuri: Mr. Chappy, who failed at the decisive point, is currently being cared for by Mr. Teshima Shigeru at the Onshi Clinic in Kuboyama, Sefuri Village, Kanzaki County, Saga Prefecture, at the foot of Mount Sefuri. When reporters drove to visit him, they saw Mr. Chappy sleeping on a temporary bed, wearing a pure wool undershirt stained with blood. Due to pain and fatigue, he kept groaning. Regarding the events at the time of the accident, he intermittently told reporters: "I arrived in Hong Kong the night before. Due to the strong wind, I couldn't depart. I departed before sunrise at 2:00 a.m. on the 19th. En route, I encountered fierce headwinds. Reaching the south of Kyushu consumed a lot of time, resulting in insufficient fuel to reach Tokyo. At 1:00 p.m. on the 19th, I arrived at Mount Sefuri and realized that there was still enough fuel. I planned to land once to replenish fuel and then depart again. Knowing that Fukuoka had a landing field, I tried my best to search, but due to the dense fog, visibility was poor. I planned to pass over Mount Sefuri when a sudden storm blew the plane down. It was not a mechanical failure that caused the crash. It was due to being attacked by the storm at the end, right above the mountain peak. Due to the fog, I couldn't see even close by. The plane had already overturned. There was no time to level it out. Finally, I collided with the mountain. It is a pity that I couldn't achieve my goal, which was only three hours away. However, it is truly unbelievable that I survived," he said. After recounting his experience, he added that his mother in France must be worried about his accident and asked to send a telegram to his mother to tell her that his injuries were not severe. (20th, Domei News Agency)

American Economic Mission Advocates Loans to China; British and French Loans Already Showing Results; China's Progress is Now Unprecedented 46

Chicago: Mr. Forbes, Chairman of the American Far East Economic Mission to China in 1935, stated to the National Convention of the International Trade Commission here today that after the Far East Economic Mission went to China to investigate, it was known that the United States needed a better credit institution in China. "I know that the United Kingdom and France have already implemented loans to China and have made considerable progress. The Chinese are also very willing for the United States to obtain this position." This matter is of great benefit to China. Under the leadership of aspiring leaders, various transportation undertakings in China have greatly developed, and the national unity is far beyond what outsiders can imagine. Japan Plans to Open Air Route in Mandated Islands; Submits Plan to League of Nations; Militarily Quite Important 47

(Geneva) Japan today submitted a plan to the League of Nations Mandate Committee to establish an air route between Japan and its mandated islands in the Pacific. Although Japan has withdrawn from the League of Nations, it still submits reports to the Mandate Committee every year because its mandated islands in the South Pacific are still under its mandate. This aviation plan is quite important because Japan's route will pass through the Pan American Airways Pacific route and the steamship route between the United States and the Philippines and Hawaii. Furthermore, it is also of great military significance. As for Japan's explanation, it is said that this air route is necessary to increase administrative efficiency and inspect fish movements. (19th, Guomin News Agency)

Japan and Germany Conclude Cultural Agreement; Same as Those Concluded with Germany and Hungary 48

(Berlin) Germany and Japan are about to sign a cultural agreement, the content of which is quite similar to those signed by Germany and Hungary. The purpose of this agreement is to enable Japan and Germany to exchange university professors and artists. Recently, Leipzig, Germany, and other major cities have held German-Japanese cultural lectures to prepare German public opinion for cultural cooperation with Japan. (19th, Hachette)

U.S. Infantry Unit Reorganization Plan; Enhance Combat Effectiveness; Experiments First Next Summer 49

(Washington) U.S. Secretary of War Mr. Woodring announced today that the Army's highest command has expressed support for the plan to reorganize the infantry unit into a more complete and active force and has scheduled experiments first next summer in preparation for final adoption. Since the last World War, there have been significant advances in weaponry and transportation, and the technical organization of the Army must undergo major changes. Mr. Woodring advocates that the number of personnel in each infantry division should be reduced from the current 22,000 to 13,500, and the number of regiments and companies should also be reduced proportionally. However, Mr. Woodring does not support increasing the current number of divisions, as none of them are close to wartime strength. (20th, Reuters)

These aircraft can accommodate three people and are well-equipped. Their engines have 850 horsepower. It is said that after the Army orders this batch of aircraft, the aircraft that should be purchased in this fiscal year have already been purchased. (19th, Reuters)

In addition to shipping large quantities of military supplies in the past week, Germany has also dispatched volunteer troops to Spain to assist in combat (the two tank vehicle teams of soldiers who went to join recently are one example). The monthly salary for these volunteer troops is very good, with ordinary soldiers receiving 500 marks and military assistants receiving 700 marks. Therefore, there is a high degree of enthusiasm for enlisting and departing. In addition, German air force pilots regard Spain as a good place to practice aerial combat, and many volunteer to go to work for the Nationalist army." Fierce Air Battle to Seize Madrid; 63 Aircraft Wreak Havoc; Ground Battles Resume After Air Battles Stop 53

Madrid: After the extremely fierce air raids on the central area of ​​Western Beijing last night, the residents of the city are all waiting for the Nationalist army to attack again today. During last night's air raid, a total of 15 three-engine Junkers bombers participated. The extent of the damage was not ascertained until dawn. Many houses were still burning, and many corpses were piled up in the ruins. A large number of civilians were bombed to death. The buildings of the Army Department, the Post Office, and the Bank of Spain were all targets of the Nationalist army's bombardment. There was a huge crater in front of the Post Office, formed by a bomb, which was as deep as six feet. During the Nationalist army's air raid, in addition to the above-mentioned bombers, there were also many fighter planes. A countless number of incendiary bombs and aerial torpedoes were dropped in the city center. Residents along Anton Martin Street all took refuge in cellars during the air raid. It is reported that they were all buried alive in the soil because the houses were destroyed and the ground collapsed. This morning, thousands of civilians fled from their destroyed houses in a state of extreme distress. According to the Reuters special correspondent stationed in the Nationalist army, the air raids by the Nationalist army were immediately followed by a major air battle. The intensity of the situation was unprecedented since the outbreak of the civil war. The correspondent claimed that although the Nationalist army's attacking aircraft had 21 bombers and 24 escorts, when each aircraft completed its bombing and was preparing to fly back, 18 aircraft from the government army side suddenly rose into the air to pursue them. At the same time, the troops of both sides fighting on the ground temporarily stopped firing, looking up at the results of the fierce air battle. Later, because the Nationalist army's bombers safely escaped, the accompanying fighter planes also stopped fighting and flew back one after another. After the air battle stopped, the land battle resumed. (20th, Reuters)

Madrid: The Defense Committee issued a communique today stating that there was a fierce battle in the university district yesterday. The government army has retaken all the buildings occupied by the Moorish troops. Only one detachment of rebels remains in the Santa Cristina College, but it has been surrounded. This morning, the rebels counterattacked and retreated with heavy losses. In yesterday's major air battle over Madrid, the government army shot down eight enemy aircraft. (20th, Reuters)

Seville: The Nationalist army broadcast a message claiming that the Nationalist army occupied the high ground of the university district today. The government army counterattacked and retreated. Most of the teams were composed entirely of foreigners. (20th, Reuters)

Fierce Bombing, Unprecedented Calamity in the Capital City, Refugees Have Nowhere to Settle 55

Madrid, Thirteen Nationalist Army aircraft flew over the capital again at 4:00 PM today, bombing the city center indiscriminately. The devastation was even more severe than before. In many places, houses were penetrated from the roof to the foundation. A bomb landed in the open space in front of the General Post Office, creating a hole two meters deep, uprooting two large trees, and shattering glass windows in the surrounding area. Another bomb landed in front of the Interior Ministry, destroying a large clock. The area around our branch office was the worst hit, with no houses within 100 meters left intact. Corpses were strewn among the rubble. Refugees on Anton Martin Street were buried alive in cellars. The bombed areas were filled with thick smoke. Thousands of residents, after this catastrophe, abandoned their homes and fled. People are living in constant fear, saying that they do not know what Madrid will look like in a few days. (Havas Dispatch, 19th)

Madrid, Special Dispatch from Our Correspondent Auchinate: It rained continuously in the city last night, and the sky was cloudy, so rebel planes were unable to come and bomb, resulting in a quiet night. This is the first time since the fighting broke out in the suburbs. Refugees in the city, unable to bear the suffering of the bombing, are leaving in droves, carrying their belongings with handcarts or shoulder poles. The defending army has requisitioned many houses in recent days to accommodate refugees. Citizens whose homes have been destroyed and have nowhere to live can go to these shelters. In small rooms that were originally only suitable for one family, more than 50 refugees are now housed. Enemy planes are bombing various areas of the city in shifts, and hardly any area is spared, so the refugee shelters often have to be moved several times a day to avoid the bombing, which is also a hardship. (Havas Dispatch, 20th)

Lisbon, According to official news from Madrid received here, more than 100 tons of explosives have fallen on the western capital in the past 24 hours. The rebels' claim that they have occupied these two places is not true. It is believed that the buildings in those two places are currently on fire. (Reuters Dispatch, 19th)

Madrid, After the capital was repeatedly bombed with incendiary bombs by Nationalist Army aircraft, it is still burning today. According to an Associated Press correspondent reporting from a mile outside the city, the houses bombed last night are still emitting black smoke, and the fires at the Montana Barracks and the Alba Palace have not been completely extinguished. A large fire has also broken out near the telephone bureau. Rebel Army Closes Ports, Britain Feels Uneasy 58

(London) After the notice from the Spanish Nationalist Army government regarding the closure of the port of Barcelona was delivered here, political figures were extremely uneasy, believing that Britain was concerned about two things: first, how to protect British interests when the Catalan coast is blockaded, and second, the general political repercussions caused by this move. Regarding the protection of British interests, the British destroyer "Gallant" is currently in the port of Barcelona, responsible for protecting the safety of British nationals in the port. The government has instructed the ship that if the port is bombarded, it should order British nationals to board the ship for refuge. In addition, the British cruiser "Arethusa" is currently sailing from Mallorca (one of the Balearic Islands belonging to Spain) to the port of Barcelona. Furthermore, British merchant ships will also be instructed by the government not to sail into the blockade area. As for the political aspect, political figures believe that the British government has not yet decided on its attitude, but the various departments of the Foreign Office are currently studying whether to issue a warning to the leader of the Spanish Nationalist Army government. Political figures also believe that what should be clarified first is whether the Nationalist Army government can actually implement the blockade. If not, and only implements a partial blockade, then its nature is extremely dangerous, and the British government will naturally oppose it. In any case, Britain currently does not recognize the two sides as belligerent entities, and therefore does not recognize the Nationalist Army authorities as having the legitimate right to declare a blockade. In short, politically, Britain will not make a decision until it has consulted with the signatory countries of the Non-Intervention Agreement, especially the French government. This consultation has not yet begun. (Havas Dispatch, 19th)

British Policy Towards the Spanish Situation Remains Unchanged, No Intention to Recognize the Rebel Army Government, Eden's Speech Favors Italy and Germany, Left-Wing Members of Parliament Shout "Shameful" 59

(London) British Foreign Secretary Eden announced in the House of Commons today the British government's attitude towards the recognition by Germany and Italy of the government established by Spanish rebel leader General Franco. The entire House listened attentively. Opposition leader Attlee rose and said that, judging from the Foreign Secretary's declaration, the British government had no intention of recognizing General Franco and his belligerent state. The Foreign Secretary said that the House should be able to distinguish between recognizing a belligerent state and recognizing any side as the Spanish government. He did not wish to say anything more on these two points. Former Naval Secretary and Labour Party member Alexander asked about reports that General Franco would blockade and bombard the port of Barcelona. The Foreign Secretary replied that Britain's position would remain in accordance with the policy established after the start of the Spanish Civil War. As for the protection of British shipping, British warships would follow the usual international practice in such incidents to defend the legitimate interests of British people. Communist Party member Gallagher asked whether Germany and Italy's announcement of recognition of the government established by General Franco was intended to undermine the Non-Intervention Agreement. The Foreign Secretary replied, "Of course not. Even if one side or the other is recognized as the government, the non-intervention policy regarding the supply of weapons can still proceed unhindered. As for undermining the agreement, there are other countries that are more deserving of blame than Germany and Italy." The Foreign Secretary continued that the information he had received on the matter was now in the hands of the members of the Non-Intervention Agreement Adjustment Committee, and there was no reason to say that the actions of the Soviet Union would render the work of the Non-Intervention Committee ineffective. (Reuters Dispatch, 19th)

(London) Foreign Secretary Eden replied to questions from several members of parliament in the House of Commons, issuing a declaration stating, "Regarding the issue of non-intervention in the Spanish Civil War, the actions of several other national governments (implicitly referring to the Soviet Union and Mexico) are worthy of criticism, and are more so than those of Germany and Italy. This is my belief, and I do not hesitate to state it firmly." When the Foreign Secretary said this, members of parliament on the right applauded in agreement, but members of parliament on the left all shouted "Shameful." (Havas Dispatch, 19th)

Anti-Revolution Case in Russia, Military Court Opened Trial Yesterday, Defendants All Plead Guilty 62

(Moscow) The first batch of Russians and foreigners recently arrested, accused of secretly engaging in espionage, sabotage, and other malicious activities, went on trial today in Novosibirsk. Among the defendants is German engineer Mr. Stickerlin, and eight other Russians, accused of sabotage in the Siberian mines, referring to the conspiracy of these people that led to the death of ten miners in the mine explosion on September 13. According to a TASS news agency, the defendants pleaded guilty during the trial and will be sentenced to death. (Reuters Dispatch, 19th)

(Moscow) The military court of the Supreme Court of the Soviet Union opened the trial on the 19th in Novosibirsk in the western Siberian region of the Trotskyist counter-revolutionary sabotage group case. The accused are Noskov, Subin, Kurov, Liachenko, Andryeev, Kovalenko, Leonenko, Bejehanov, and Sticklin (German engineer).

According to the indictment read by the court, "Since 1935, the accused have been active members of a special counter-revolutionary sabotage group, operating in the Kemelovo minefield, with the aim of harming the Soviet state through various conspiracies and sabotage methods. Between 1935 and 1936, they repeatedly committed crimes in an organized manner, attempting to disrupt the mine management system, disrupt coal mining work, destroy the mine's transportation system, and damage the mine's safety equipment and work regulations, leading to the danger of gas." All the defendants were defended by members of the Novosibirsk Bar Association. It is reported that all the defendants have unanimously confessed to the crimes they are accused of. (TASS Dispatch, 20th)

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek Arrives in Shandong for Inspection, Stays for About Three Hours, Then Flies Back to Luoyang from Jinan 70

Jinan Correspondence: Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of the Military Affairs Commission flew to Jinan from Luoyang on the 19th for inspection, arriving in Jinan at noon. He stayed for about three hours, and at 3:30 PM, he flew back to Luoyang on the same plane. Before Chairman Chiang Kai-shek came to Shandong from Luoyang, a telegram arrived in Jinan the day before, instructing Han Fuju not to alarm various circles, and that leaders of various agencies do not need to participate in the welcome. Therefore, at 9:00 AM on the 19th, Han Fuju and his wife went to Zhangzhuang Airport to welcome him. The only other people who arrived were Provincial Government Committee Member Zhang Yue, Public Security Bureau Chief Zhao Guangpei, and Zhangzhuang Garrison Brigade Commander Rong Guangxing. At the same time, they went from the Provincial Government to Zhangzhuang, and temporary military police and security teams were stationed along the way to provide security. At about 12:00 PM, two planes flew in from the west, and at 12:15 PM, they landed at the airport. Chiang Kai-shek was in the first plane, and his entourage was in the second plane. Those who came with Chiang Kai-shek were Qian Dajun and more than ten others. Han Fuju and others approached the plane to welcome him and pay their respects. After Chiang Kai-shek got off the plane, he thanked Han Fuju and exchanged greetings, and then took cars to the Provincial Government. At 12:50 PM, Chiang Kai-shek, Han Fuju, and others arrived at the Provincial Government and went to the Chairman's office to rest and talk. Li Shuchun, Director of the Civil Affairs Department of Shandong Province, Zhang Honglie, Director of the Construction Department, He Siyuan, Director of the Education Department, Zhang Shaotang, Secretary-General, Cao Fulin, Division Commander, Liu Shuxiang, Chief of Staff of the Headquarters, Zhang Yue of the Provincial Committee, Wu Zhenzan, President of the High Court, and Li Wenzhai, member of the Provincial Party Department, and many others had heard the news and arrived at the Provincial Government to welcome him. Chiang Kai-shek received them in the office and inquired about the situation of the Party and government. After talking for five minutes, all the dignitaries withdrew, and Chiang Kai-shek and Han Fuju continued to talk in the office, inquiring about the military and political affairs of Shandong Province. Han Fuju answered one by one. They had lunch together in the office, while Qian Dajun and others were entertained by Liu Shuxiang in another room. At 3:00 PM, after finishing lunch, Chiang Kai-shek said goodbye to the Provincial Government and took a car to Zhangzhuang Airport. When he arrived at Zhangzhuang, it was already 3:30 PM. Han Fuju and all the members of the Provincial Government, the members of the Provincial Party Department, and the military and political leaders all went to the airport to see him off. Chiang Kai-shek and Qian Dajun and others took the same plane back to Luoyang, and Han Fuju and others dispersed and returned. According to sources, Chiang Kai-shek's visit to Jinan was to inspect the local situation and inquire about political party affairs, and there were no other tasks. Chiang Kai-shek expressed his satisfaction with the political construction of Shandong Province. (19th)

Qingdao Circles Vigorously Support Suiyuan, Over Two Thousand Yuan Already Remitted to the Front Lines, Continued Fundraising Underway 71

Qingdao Correspondence: The soldiers of Suiyuan are defending the country, bravely fighting the enemy in the icy and snowy land. The news has spread, inspiring the entire nation to vow to be their support. Therefore, people from all over are donating to support Suiyuan like a rising storm, showing that the spirit of the people is not dead. In addition to organizing a large-scale comfort mission for the soldiers at the front, all circles in Qingdao have also been actively donating. Over two thousand yuan has been remitted to the front lines in recent days. The details of donations from various circles are summarized below:

Shandong University

Since the students of the National Shandong University in this city organized the Suiyuan Anti-Japanese Support Association, they have been actively fundraising. Teachers, students, and staff of the entire school have donated over 1,500 yuan. It is scheduled to be remitted to Suiyuan through the JinCheng Bank on the 19th, along with a telegram of condolence to the anti-Japanese soldiers at the front. The text of the telegram reads: "To Chairman Fu of Suiyuan and forwarded to all the soldiers at the front: The bandits and puppets are committing crimes and acting as accomplices for the enemy. Looking north to the clouds of the frontier, the whole country is filled with indignation. Our soldiers at the front are defending the territory with bloodshed and vowing to resist the enemy to the death, inspiring all our compatriots. The safety of Suiyuan is related to the overall situation. We urge you to strictly organize your troops, sweep away the enemy's forces, block the enemy's ambitions, and secure the border. Our association has launched a fundraising campaign to assist the soldiers defending the territory at the front, to express our sincere intentions. In addition to the funds being remitted separately, we send this telegram of condolence and await news of victory. The National Shandong University Suiyuan Anti-Japanese Support Association kowtows."

Various Primary and Secondary Schools

On the 17th of this month, the principals of various middle schools in this city held a joint meeting. It was decided that each school principal, teacher, and staff member should donate at least one day's income, and each middle school student should also go home to solicit donations from their families, with each student donating at least 20 cents. On the 18th, the principals of all elementary schools in the city also held a meeting, deciding that the donation method for each elementary school principal, teacher, and staff member would follow the method of the middle schools, and each elementary school student should also go home to solicit donations from their families, with each student donating at least 10 cents.

Autonomous Committee

The deputy chairman of the Autonomous Preparatory Committee of this city, Yuan Daochong, and others, in view of the daily urgency of foreign aggression, should each do their best to support the soldiers defending the country if they cannot serve on the battlefield. They have initiated a fundraising campaign to comfort the soldiers at the front. Mr. Yuan took the lead by donating his entire month's salary of 300 yuan, and other staff members also actively donated, raising a total of 550 yuan. The donation has been handed over to the bank to be remitted to Chairman Fu to show condolences. The telegram sent by Mr. Yuan and others to Chairman Fu reads: "China is unfortunate to have traitors and villains who act as accomplices for the enemy, betray the country, and destroy its own defenses. Now Suiyuan is taking the brunt. Fortunately, your troops are loyal, brave, and indignant, fighting in the icy and snowy land, resisting tigers and wolves, standing as the vanguard of the whole country, showing the people the importance of humanitarian defense, and letting friendly countries and even enemy countries know that the spirit of the Chinese people is not dead. This is of utmost importance, not just for eliminating the enemy and protecting the territory. Daochong and others are ashamed of our insignificance, unable to serve on the battlefield. We sincerely wish you victory and enclose 550 yuan of national currency, entrusted to the Tianjin Dagongbao for forwarding, to provide some assistance for rewarding the meritorious and comforting the wounded. We know that this is a mere drop in the bucket, but we offer it as a way to return to the country what we have accumulated through blood and sweat, and to seek peace of mind. We humbly offer this sincere intention and hope that you will take it into consideration."

Other Circles

The Postal Workers' Union of this city donated 100 yuan, which was remitted to the front lines the day before yesterday. The President of the Local Court of this city, Mai Dinghua, has also announced to all judicial officials that they will donate to comfort the Suiyuan soldiers who are killing the enemy, and he has taken the lead by donating 30 yuan to promote this. Each judge will donate 10 yuan, each clerk 5 yuan, and each worker 1 yuan. Once a certain amount has been collected, it will be remitted to the front lines. In addition, the Red Swastika Society, the Lianqing Society, the Youth Association, and other organizations in this city are planning to launch a fundraising association and perform traditional Chinese opera to solicit donations from all circles. The results in the future are expected to be considerable.

Hankou Correspondence: After the unfortunate death of the late Chairman Yang of Hubei Province from an assassination, the funeral ceremony was extremely grand. Starting from the 19th, the public memorial service will be held at Mr. Yang's mourning hall in the Provincial Library. The Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, various ministries and departments, and the governments of various provinces have all sent representatives to preside over the memorial service. Relying on you as a shield, we looked forward to saving the country together. Heaven did not spare you, and you suffered a sudden death. The pillars and beams have collapsed, which is not only a personal pain. Your legacy still exists, and who will share the administration? The country has high rewards, and only you deserve them. We respectfully offer this mourning sacrifice, and may your spirit rest here. Accept this offering." You went to the front lines and deployed troops in the Jiangdian region. You had brilliant plans and stood out independently. We hoped to work together to save the country, and I dared to serve as your subordinate. You were loyal, clear, and diligent, and your achievements were presented well. You excelled in handling affairs and were capable in all aspects. You responded to all tasks and worked diligently from dawn to dusk. You examined the truth and went straight to the point. You were as straight as a line, not afraid of being slandered, and not self-congratulatory. Knowing your sincerity, you worked hard for the country. The Yangtze and Han rivers in the south, your command was exemplary. Your reputation spread with your political achievements, and the people were happy to obey your orders. With extraordinary plans and meritorious service, you suddenly suffered a cruel attack. Thinking of your ambition and loyalty, you were unparalleled. The country has lost its pillar, and this is not only a personal sorrow. Cherishing your efforts, your plans will shine forever. The nine heavens can be reached, but tears cannot be stopped. Your merits will be rewarded and your burial will be grand. The mountains and peaks stand tall, praising your lofty character. Your reputation for integrity and love will be admired for a thousand years. I offer this cup of wine to you, and I am filled with sadness in the wind. Alas, alas, alas, accept this offering." (4) Provincial Government Committee Eulogy: On November 19, 25th year of the Republic of China, Lu Zhu, Meng Guangpeng, Jia Shiyi, Cheng Qibao, Liu Shoupeng, Li Shucheng, Fan Xiji, Wu Guozhen, Director of the Security Department Ding Bingquan, Deputy Director Jin Jutang, and all staff members of the Hubei Provincial Government respectfully offer this sacrifice to the spirit of the late Chairman Yang, saying: Mr. Yang, lofty and upright, soaring alone, sharp and capable, wise and resolute, establishing government in the land of Chu, continuing the legacy of the sages, with virtue comparable to Yang Hu, and strictness comparable to Tao Kan. From the beginning of his administration, he first clarified official standards, removing abuses and promoting benefits. Gentle but not submissive, strong but not overbearing, diligently seeking the people's welfare, and advancing without hesitation. Reforming the mind and changing customs, with unflinching sound arguments, elucidating the arts of governance, and creating a golden rule. Guiding and showing the way to colleagues, a mentor to all. When his ambition was about to be fulfilled, he followed these precepts. But like an orchid that is fragrant and broken, or a jade that is tight and broken, things are jealous of firmness and fragrance, and people dislike brightness and purity. The world's praise and criticism, what do they mean to you? Your illustrious achievements have already been immortalized. The days we spent together are still memorable. Zichan has no successors, who will enrich the town? With this we endure our sorrow, respectfully offer this sacrifice, pour the wine, and gaze with tears and sighs. Accept this offering." Baoshan All Circles Support Suiyuan Conference 73

All circles in Baoshan County have scheduled a conference for all circles to support Suiyuan's suppression of bandits and soldiers on the 20th at the county government conference hall. Many important proposals were decided, including fundraising to comfort the front lines and passing a resolution to comfort the soldiers at the front. In addition, prisoners in Baoshan County Prison and Detention Center also voluntarily fasted for one day on the 20th, requesting the county government to transfer the money saved to the front lines.

Songjiang Prison Inmates Fast to Save the Country 74

The entire group of inmates in this county's prison, alarmed by the daily urgency of the national crisis and the siege of Suiyuan by the puppet bandits, believe that as fellow citizens, they have a duty to save the nation during this critical time of survival. They voluntarily stopped eating for one day to transfer the funds to donate to the government for purchasing aircraft, thereby expressing their patriotic enthusiasm. After submitting the request to the prison warden, who then forwarded it to the county government for approval, the county government issued an order stating that the inmates, despite being imprisoned, still had enthusiastic patriotism and were willing to fast to donate for the purchase of aircraft, which was commendable. However, considering that the inmates' daily nutrition was not sufficient, fasting for one day would be detrimental to their health, so they were advised to reduce their food in installments to make up for one day's worth of food. The inmates were delighted after receiving the order and wished to fast for one day on the 21st of this month instead of reducing their food in installments. However, the prison warden, out of concern for the inmates' health, purchased rice and cooked porridge at his own expense to feed the inmates on that day.

Wuxi Jiang Zuobin Comes to Xixi to Inspect 75

Minister of Interior Jiang Zuobin, in order to understand the actual situation of administration in various provinces and cities, arrived in Zhenjiang from Beijing on the 18th to inspect the various bureaus and offices of the provincial capital. He then departed by car from the province to Danyang and Jintan, and then to Wujin, inspecting the county administration of the counties he passed through, and inspecting the police force. On the evening of the 19th, at 6 p.m., he arrived in Wuxi from Changzhou. Those who accompanied Mr. Jiang to Wuxi included Liu Fu, Chief Secretary of the Ministry of Interior, Jiang Tianqing, Section Chief of the Administrative Division, Yu Xiuhao, Yang Junli, Section Chief of the Civil Affairs Division, as well as translators and guards. Yesterday morning, Mr. Jiang inspected the various administrative agencies such as the Commissioner's Office and the County Government. Mr. Jiang's mission on this tour is to inspect the local administration, public security facilities, mass training, baojia system, and land administration of various provinces and counties, as well as to inspect the local security teams and police teams, assess their performance, and study improvements in order to achieve perfection. Mr. Jiang is scheduled to first inspect the six provinces of Jiangsu, Anhui, Jiangxi, Zhejiang, Hunan, and Hubei within 20 days, and then return to Beijing to schedule inspections of the provinces of Sichuan, Yunnan, Guizhou, Guangdong, and Fujian.

Fire Burns Down Entire Village 76

In Xiliu Lane in Taifu Township near Anzhen in the seventh district of the county, there are more than ten households, mostly farmers. The other night around 8 p.m., a fire suddenly broke out at the home of Hua A'er due to carelessness. By the time it was discovered, it had already broken through the roof and spread rapidly, making it difficult to extinguish. It spread to the homes of neighbors Li A'wu, Shi Genpei, and others. The fire brigades of the east and west sections of Anzhen heard the alarm and immediately drove to the scene to bravely fight the fire. It took about two hours to extinguish the fire, but all the houses in the village had been reduced to ashes. When the fire was raging, a newborn baby in a farmer's household was buried in the fire because it was too late to rescue it. For a time, the cries of sorrow and grief spread across the fields, a scene too tragic to witness. Afterwards, all the villagers were homeless, hungry, and cold, making it difficult to survive. The Baozhang of Fenghu Lane, Gu Xueli, and others took the initiative to propose raising donations for relief to temporarily sustain their lives.

"Youth News" Complimentary Subscription 77

The cultural circles of Wuxi, in view of the high standards and prices of various publications in Shanghai, which cannot meet the needs of the inland, have issued a low-level publication with a very low price and content that strives to be popular. It is published every Saturday for a total of forty issues per year. Since its founding in September, it has been published to the eleventh issue. The content is divided into various types, including random thoughts on current affairs, national affairs, world trends, special commentaries on current affairs, local communications, social thoughts, popular talks, and youth groups. It is laid out in the format of a small newspaper, which is very exquisite and pleasing to the eye. The annual subscription is 60 cents. For five copies or more, each copy is only 40 cents. Half a year is 20 cents. Since its publication, the publication has expanded from the Beijing-Shanghai line to the provinces of Shandong, Henan, Fujian, and Guangdong. It is now seeking opinions from readers to make improvements and has a special free subscription method. Just send a letter to the Youth News on the Wuxi Library Road and you will receive a free subscription.

Yangzhou Large Number of Bandit Ships Seized 78

According to confidential reports, the Jiangdu Anti-Smuggling Team received information that water bandits were entrenched in Erjiangying and other places in the third district. Deputy Captain Zhang Qingan led detectives Zhai Jingwu, Xue Zhiming, and eight others to investigate and suppress the bandits. They discovered multiple bandit ships successively at the mouth of the river in Sanjiangying and at the Shuangjiangkou area in Yangzhou County. The ships raised their sails and attempted to escape. The deputy captain led the detectives to hire boats to pursue them. The bandits resisted on the river, and the two sides fought for several hours. When the distance between them was close, the deputy captain led the detectives to bravely jump onto the bandit ships. They confiscated three box cannons, twenty-six bullets, and three carbines with twelve rows of bullets from the bandits. One of the carbines was thrown into the river by the bandits. The bandits Sun Yonglong, Jin Guangren, Zhang Qicai, Zhou Jinniu, Ye Dechang, Zhou Jinfa, Gao Hongxi, Zhou Wanqing, Zhou Changjin, Dai Xiaoshizi, and Sun Baofu, a total of eleven people, along with eleven bandit ships, thirteen family members of the bandits (women), and a dozen boys and girls, were all captured. That night, they were handed over to Wang Ming, the captain of the He Kou Zhuang Ding Reserve Team, to assist in guarding them. This morning (19th), they were transported by the Longzhen bus of the Yangzhou Company to Huoqiao. In addition to handing over the bandit ships and bandit family members to the Huoqiao Security Regiment for guarding, the deputy captain and eleven bandit criminals, five rifles, and bullets were transported by car from Huoqiao to Yangzhou for interrogation to determine how to handle the case.

Fire in Qinglongshan, Mingzhong Township, Cinan 83

Xu Haofeng, a resident of Qinglongshan, Mingzhong Township, Cinan, is a farmer who is diligent and frugal, and his family is well-off. Unexpectedly, at 4 p.m. on the 17th, a fire suddenly broke out in his firewood shed. Because the area is mountainous and there are few people to provide assistance, they had to let the fire spread until it was extinguished around 11 p.m. It is estimated that 47 houses were burned down, more than 40,000 catties of rice and grain were lost, and eight houses were demolished, resulting in losses of 50,000 to 60,000 yuan, a truly huge robbery.

Wuhu One-Day Movement in the Electrical Industry 84

Mr. Shen Sifang, General Manager of Wuhu Mingyuan Electrical Company, believes that the movement of contributing one day to the country is the bounden duty of citizens to save the country and survive. If all compatriots across the country can contribute one day's income to the country to enrich national defense construction, the effect will be significant. Recently, the National Federation of Private Electrical Industries held its eighth member representative conference in Beijing. Mr. Shen made a temporary motion requesting the national electrical industry to jointly hold it. The method is to take the company's one-day operating income, deduct all expenses, and contribute it to the country. On the employee side, they are encouraged to contribute all of their one-day salary income. It was decided and approved. It is reported that Mingyuan Company has implemented it on the 13th of this month. In addition to deducting expenses from the operating income of 200 yuan in national currency, all employees voluntarily contributed their one-day salary income of 165 yuan, 2 dimes, and 3 cents in national currency to the country. The money will be sent to the Wuhu County Chamber of Commerce to be forwarded to the National Government National Defense Committee.

Hangzhou Dangerous Situation of the Hangping Seawall 85

The Hangping section of the Shuogan et al. seawall is showing a dangerous situation as the seawall is shifting outwards. The Construction Department has specially dispatched Zhou Zhenlun, director of the Water Conservancy Engineering Office, to conduct an on-site inspection. He returned to Hangzhou on the evening of the 19th. According to reports, a hundred meters of the Shuogan seawall is not only shifting outwards, but also because the silt outside the seawall has recently been eroded by huge tides, the bottom of the seawall is hollow, and the seawall is leaning outwards, teetering on the verge of collapse. If repairs are not carried out quickly, once the tide rises, the seawall will inevitably be washed away, and the Shanghai-Hangzhou highway along the seawall is also in danger of being cut off. It is now planned to apply to the provincial government for an allocation of 100,000 yuan for major repairs and reconstruction of the stone seawall to protect it.

Sino-American Association and American Chamber of Commerce Held a Grand Banquet Last Night, Chairmen Franking and Guo Bingwen Gave Speeches, Performed Wireless Radio Communication with the Plane, and Wang Xiaolai and Three Others Gave Speeches in the Plane 86

The Sino-American Trade Association and the American Chamber of Commerce, in order to expand Sino-American trade and enhance Sino-American relations, held a grand joint banquet last night at the American Club. Franking, representative of the Sino-American Trade Association and President of the American Chamber of Commerce, gave a speech. Wang Xiaolai, Arnold, Danegee, Xu Maigan, and others performed wireless radio communication from an airplane. The sound was clear and audible throughout the venue. At 10 o'clock, there were magic shows and trade films, and the event ended joyfully at 12 o'clock late at night. The details are recorded as follows:

Venue Decoration

The entire fifth floor of the American Club at 209 Fuzhou Road was decorated with red silk banners with the words "Sino-American Co-prosperity," "International Harmony," and "Exchange of Goods." The doors and windows were decorated with colorful silk fabrics, creating a magnificent atmosphere.

Attending Chairmen

The grand banquet yesterday was attended by Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce; Peng Xuepei, Director of the Ministry of Communications; Wen Yuqing, Director of the Aviation Department; Cai Jingjun, Director of the Public Security Bureau; Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau; Xu Peihuang, Director of the Public Utilities Bureau; Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce; Du Yuesheng, Chairman of the Local Association; Danegee, General Manager of China Aviation Corporation; Zheng Lai, Director of the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance; Yu Qiaqing, General Manager of Sanbei Company; Gosh, American Consul General; Stantung, Administrative Consul; Hillmeck, Inspector; Arnold, Commercial Counselor; Pallas, Commander of the U.S. Marine Corps; Tan Dewei, Manager of China Electric Company; Franking, President of the American Chamber of Commerce; Directors Feichemai, Hubujin, Kelilai, Graufuo, Feiste, Tugu De, Folimen, Pan Jin, Yadan Shi, Oermen, Jierlan, Makai; Guo Bingwen, Jin Runxiang, Bei Songsun, Directors of the Sino-American Trade Association; Miao Zhongxiu, General Manager; and Wu Yunzhai, Shou Jingwei, Xu Xinliu, and others, totaling more than 300 people.

Aviation Communication

The Sino-American guests were seated at 8:15 PM. Around 9 PM, Franking, President of the American Chamber of Commerce, stood up and requested Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce; Arnold, Commercial Counselor of the United States; Danegee, General Manager of China Aviation Corporation; and Xu Maigan, Manager of Chase Bank, to leave their seats and go by car to Longhua Airport, board a China Aviation Corporation airplane, and fly around the city. At 9:30 PM, Tan Dewei, Manager of China Electric Company, shouted to Franking, and then Arnold in the plane communicated with Franking at the venue. Then Wang Xiaolai in the plane communicated with Tan Dewei at the venue (Wang's speech is below). Finally, Danegee and Xu Maigan in the plane talked with Wen Yuqing and others at the venue. The sound was clear and audible throughout the venue.

Wang Xiaolai's Speech

Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, said in his speech: "Today is the 151st anniversary of Sino-American trade and commerce. I am very honored to speak here. China and the United States are two great republics, located in the eastern and western hemispheres. In these 151 years, we have established a very friendly relationship. We know that 'friendship' is the foundation of everything, especially in the fundamental meaning of trade. Of course, there is a need, but if there are many people supplying the need, then the buyers and sellers will definitely choose to trade with those with whom they have always had a good friendship. There is a Chinese saying, 'Good comes and good goes,' which means that if someone comes with good intentions, they will definitely leave with good intentions. But the so-called good intentions are not just words, they must plant a seed of good intentions in everyone's heart. In the past, there was a debate between Gongsun Longzi and Kong Chuan. Gongsun Longzi said that chickens have three legs, and Kong Chuan said that chickens have only two legs. The result of the debate was that Gongsun Longzi won. For example, all tools, even if they have legs, cannot walk, which is enough to prove it. But Kong Chuan said, 'Gongsun Longzi can win people's mouths, but not their hearts.' Winning people's mouths, though winning, is useless. Winning people's hearts allows the good intentions in their hearts to direct their hands to take the money earned from sweat and blood to buy goods. In the past, China and the United States did indeed plant such good intentions in each other's hearts. I hope that these good intentions will grow longer and prosper, and that we can cultivate these good intentions throughout the world, and that China and the United States can build this foundation."

Chairman's Speech

After Wang Xiaolai and the other three left their seats, Franking, President of the American Chamber of Commerce, stood up and gave a speech, welcoming and introducing the distinguished guests. He decided to have Guo Bingwen, Chairman of the International Trade Bureau, represent the Sino-American Trade Association and give a speech in English. He said, in brief, "The purpose of tonight's meeting is to enhance Sino-American friendship and develop Sino-American trade. Representatives of the two countries are gathered here, which is a great event. We cannot help but think of the 150-year history of Sino-American relations, and what runs through it is sincerity and friendship. This pleasant history is the result of mutual understanding and trust. In general, for countries to have smooth trade relations, they must be based on mutual harmony. How to further promote the development of Sino-American friendship and promote political, cultural, and economic relations is a common obligation of the people of both countries. In this era, economic nationalism is prevalent, and countries are vying to set up various trade barriers. In fact, no independent country can do without mutual assistance. This is especially true for China and the United States, because China is an important consumer of American goods, and the United States is also a major customer of China. (Recently, the United States has ranked first in China's foreign trade.) The American economic recovery movement is underway, and China's national economic construction movement is also just beginning. In the future, the increase in the purchasing power of the two countries and the expansion of the volume of trade are expected. However, we must remember that although emotion and purchasing power are important factors in international trade, the success of trade cannot rely solely on emotional factors, nor can it only depend on the purchasing power of its people. International trade is often the goal of international competition. If China wants to maintain the American market, it must strive to improve its products. Conversely, if the United States wants to expand trade with China, its traders must be able to provide more favorable terms to Chinese merchants. If these conditions can be fully realized, the future of Sino-American trade will be even more brilliant."

Entertainment Performances

After the chairman's speech, Gosh, the American Consul General, and others also gave speeches. The speeches were long and omitted for brevity. At 10:10 PM, McLeana, a world-renowned magician, began to perform various novel magic tricks to add to the fun. At 10:50 PM, trade films were shown, and the event ended joyfully at 12:00 midnight.

Accordingly, I am writing to request that you check and inform the bureaus and announce it to the residents of the area. Approved, and ordered to inform all bureaus and announce to residents.

It was decided to hold a joint meeting at 4:00 PM today at the Hong Kong Road Bank Club. They will submit the opinions on income tax from banks of banking associations in various places, member banks, and money shops of money industry associations in various places for research.

Representative of Dutch Sugar, Stoker, Expresses That There is Absolutely No Request to Reduce Sugar Tax, Met with Liang Hejun of the Sugar Management Committee and Stated in Person, Sugar Industry Association Held a Meeting Yesterday to Report to Avoid Misunderstandings 93

According to the New Voice News Agency, Mr. Stoker, representative of the Dutch Java Sugar Sales Office, arrived in Shanghai a few days ago to investigate the sugar sales situation in China. A few days ago, he met with Chairman Liang of the Sugar Transportation and Sales Management Committee of the Ministry of Finance, and the association officially stated on behalf of the Dutch sugar industry that the previous Western newspaper reported that Dutch sugar merchants and a certain country's sugar industry had signed an agreement to change the Chinese sugar industry market and jointly requested the Chinese government to reduce the import tax on foreign sugar. It is completely false and there is no such thing. Fearing that it would cause misunderstandings among Chinese sugar merchants, he asked Liang to convey this to the sugar merchants. Therefore, at 4:00 PM yesterday, Chairman Liang specifically convened the directors of the China National Sugar Production and Sales Association at the meeting to convey this situation and asked them to inform sugar merchants across the country to avoid misunderstandings. It can be proved that the Western newspaper's report is untrue, and the sugar tax will not change, which is even more firm. Sugar merchants across the country can also operate with peace of mind.

Enthusiastic Support for Suiyuan from All Circles 94

One-Dollar Movement: The First Special District City Federation is promoting a One-Dollar Aid Suiyuan movement. The implementation measures are as follows: (1) The Federation will send letters to various agencies and groups in the city, requesting them to organize it uniformly; (2) The Federation will send telegrams to the whole country to organize it uniformly; (3) Each member of the Federation and members of its branches will be given "One Dollar" receipts prepared by the Federation and sent to solicit donations. After a certain amount is collected, it will be transferred to the bank designated by the Suiyuan Bandit Suppression Relief and Rescue Committee of this city for collection; (4) Donations from various agencies, groups, and citizens participating in the One-Dollar Movement will be sent to the bank designated by the Suiyuan Bandit Suppression Relief and Rescue Committee of this city for collection; (5) Newspapers can also collect donations, but please indicate "One-Dollar Aid Suiyuan Movement"; (6) Donations from members of the Federation and its branches are limited to one week. If there are any omissions, please send them directly to the bank designated by the Suiyuan Bandit Suppression Relief and Rescue Committee of this city afterwards; (7) For member stores that have already donated, a "One-Dollar Aid Suiyuan Movement has been donated" paper strip will be given to be posted at the entrance to avoid duplication; (8) The expenses for printing receipts and various publicity materials will be paid from the Federation's funds and cannot be used for donations. The Federation is also promoting the "One-Dollar Aid Suiyuan Movement" and has sent a special telegram to all agencies, groups, and schools across the country to promote it. The original telegram stated, "The bandits and puppets are invading the border, and the situation is serious. Fortunately, Chairman Suiyuan Chuan and all the soldiers are fighting bravely, but they have not yet succeeded. However, the bandits and puppets are acting recklessly, and their background is obvious. To kill the enemy and achieve results, we must rely on substantial support. Since September 18th, our territory has been shrinking day by day, and Suiyuan has become the only barrier for the country. In terms of the situation, Suiyuan is the gateway to North China. If there is any mistake, the enemy will drive straight in, and the whole country will be in danger. Therefore, the bandit and puppet invasion of Suiyuan is by no means a local war, but a continued step in the enemy's plan to destroy China. We must concentrate the strength of the whole country and rise up to rescue it. Everyone should recognize that saving Suiyuan is saving the country, and saving the people of Suiyuan is saving ourselves. The situation is urgent, and we must not wait and see any longer. Moreover, in this cold winter season, the north is a frozen and snowy land, the disaster victims are starving, and the soldiers are suffering from the cold, urgently awaiting rescue. Therefore, this Federation has launched the 'One-Dollar Aid Suiyuan Movement,' hoping that all compatriots across the country will make a great wish to save the country and enthusiastically donate, and use the collected funds to comfort the soldiers on the front lines and the disaster victims. However, the movement to save the country is not limited to one place, so this telegram is sent to convey the main points of the 'One-Dollar Aid Suiyuan Movement,' respectfully requesting you to lead your subordinates, awaken the people, and promote it uniformly to encourage morale and save the country from danger." Furthermore, the Federation, in view of the increasingly serious Sui border war, and at the same time, a certain party transported a large number of poison gas bombs and poison gas launchers from Dolun, preparing to release poison gas against us, deeply feels that purchasing gas masks and transporting them to the front lines is more urgent than providing winter clothing such as gloves. After a proposal by Federation member Li BieKui, it was decided to launch a mass campaign to collect gas masks so that the patriotic soldiers on the front lines can be fearless.

A preparatory committee will be established within the shortest possible time to start everything. In the first step, it is planned to set up forty companies. As for the banking sector, it is planned to raise 4 million yuan to invest in the company, and the negotiations have been completed.
