Women's Special Issue: How Can One Be a Modern Woman? By Tong Yizhen

Do we dress in 20th-century fashion, carry a few foreign books, or confidently rattle off something or other, and then consider ourselves modern women? No, these are not the crucial questions. To be modern women, we must first approach with a sincere attitude, reflecting on and examining the past, alerting and encouraging the future, and making strong resolutions and efforts to practice the following basic conditions:

1. Sound Physique

Compared to the physiques of people in Europe and America, we Chinese people feel some fear and shame. This is especially true for us women, and the difference is even more significant. Alas! We can only blame ourselves for not being good in the past, for being infected with the residual poison of being "frail" and having "willow waists and golden lotuses." As a result, we have reached this terrible phenomenon. We must strive to break free from the shackles of near-death and fight against nature. To be modern women, we must first possess the strength of a lion!

2. Simple Habits

I believe no one can deny that our women's desire for luxury is indeed much greater than that of others. When we look at the customs reports on the import numbers of perfumes and cosmetics, how disheartening they are! In this autumn of national crisis, we bear the responsibility for the rise and fall of the country, and we are busy and inseparable, yet we add a huge leak to the national economy. How can we be worthy of our motherland? To be modern women, we should no longer be as flamboyantly decorated as flowers. Although "the love of beauty is in everyone's nature," what we need is simple beauty. We must recognize that perfumes, cosmetics, and all decorative items are only for outdated people. We should abandon these things far away.

3. Independent Spirit

For decades, we have been shouting "freedom and equality" every day. Although we have gained the sympathy of some people, we are still heavily oppressed in reality. The most fundamental reason we seek is that economic independence is not possible. Because from ancient times to the present, we have been poisoned by the dependence of "marrying a chicken and following a chicken, marrying a dog and following a dog." To be modern women, we must have an independent spirit. No one can rely on anyone else to seek true "freedom and equality!"

Finally, I hope all female compatriots in the country will become modern women and shoulder the mission of saving the country and seeking survival!

A Unique Woman in American Journalism By Caoshi

America is a paradise for women. Anything a man can do, a woman can do as well. However, the job of "war correspondent," which is the most demanding, and requires facing death and enduring countless dangers, seems unsuitable for women due to the environment and their inherent nature. Unexpectedly, in 1914, when the European War was just beginning, Margarita Evira MUGARRIETA, the daughter of the first Mexican consul in San Francisco, who was a woman's magazine reporter, secretly disguised herself as a man named Mr. Jack Bee GARLAND. At the age of 35, she went to the European Western Front, personally went deep into the front lines within the fire line, to collect war reports, in order to complete the mission of a special correspondent for a major American news conglomerate. Garland's intention was deeply rooted in the belief that the scope of women's magazines was too small, and that it was not enough to smoothly pursue a lifetime career. She took advantage of the good opportunity of the European War to express her ambitions and pursue a more distant and greater ambition. Afterwards, when the European War ended, Mr. Garland returned to the country in a flamboyant manner, wearing a high collar, smoking large cigars, and driving a small car, frequenting bars where male reporters gathered. For 22 years, no one had ever uncovered her true identity. She has written articles on the war in Africa against the Rif people against Spain, the dispute between the two South American countries of Peru and Bolivia, and the recent Italian expedition to the African country of Ethiopia. Her person has long been proven in the field, and has become an expert in war affairs in the journalism field. Everyone knows that he is Mr. Garland, who is very knowledgeable, and has long developed a natural tendency. It was not until Mr. Garland passed away in early September of this year that his close friend, Miss George SHADBURNE, revealed his special behavior. This is truly an unprecedented secret in American news history, similar to the words of novelists and myths.

It is said that Ms. Huang Nuting, the daughter of Huang Jieqing, the former acting Spanish envoy to our country, also dressed as a man, following the example of the unique people in the American news industry. Could it be said to be one of a kind?

The Physique of Japan's Maehata By Jiyun

The Japanese swimmer Hideshi Maehata, who returned from the World Games, displayed her amazing performance in Berlin, leaving hundreds of thousands of spectators with a good impression of Japanese women's sports. She not only lived up to the hard work of her daily practice, but also completed her mission. Not to mention women, even men, being diligent in sports is enough to develop their physique. Conversely, amazing athletic achievements must have amazing physiques. The physical fitness of our country's athletes who attended the World Games has already lagged behind. It is more shameful that the results of this sport are poor. Except for specialized gymnastics schools, girls' schools not only do not pay attention to the students' sports, but can be said to have no regard for the physical fitness of girls. The physical examination during the entrance examination is also just a formality. How many physical education instructors pay attention to whether the students' physical fitness is improving or declining? The general public's observation of women's physical fitness only focuses on the beauty of curves and the beauty of the human body. If they are not slender and graceful, they are round and plump, which is fundamentally wrong. In this extremely difficult national situation, we do not need the physical fitness of movie stars and dance queens, but only truly healthy women to be the mothers of small citizens in the future.

After Hideshi Maehata returned from the World Games, Ms. Shigeyo Takeuchi examined her physique and discovered amazing results. Her height is 1.602 meters, which is taller than the average height of Japanese men. (The average height of Japanese men is longest between the ages of 30 and 35, only 1.60 meters.) Her weight is 58.5 kilograms, which is also heavier than men (the average weight of Japanese men is heaviest between the ages of 40 and 45, 57 kilograms). Her chest circumference is 90.48 centimeters, her shoulder width is 41.2 centimeters, her waist width is 29.3 centimeters, and her skin thickness is 1.4 centimeters. Her lower limb length is 85 centimeters, her back muscle strength is 108 kilograms, her arm span is 1.668 meters, her lung capacity is 4,000 cubic centimeters, and her chest circumference ratio is 58 kilograms.

The characteristics of Maehata's physique are that her arm span is 10 centimeters longer than the standard, her lung capacity is almost twice that of ordinary people, and her back muscle strength is 20 kilograms stronger than her total muscle strength. The chest circumference ratio is the ratio of chest circumference to height, and this is what Japanese women lack compared to Western women. The standard chest circumference ratio for Western women is 55%, and Maehata has now surpassed it. Although not all Japanese women have this kind of special and excellent physique like Maehata, perhaps our Chinese women have never had this kind of healthy physique. But generally speaking, the physical fitness of women in China and Japan is very different. Because women in our country do not pay attention to exercise on weekdays, their physical fitness cannot develop. Not only is there no hope for excellent sports results, but even domestic affairs, labor service, production and education are all significantly affected. Readers can understand this after comparing their own or their children's physical fitness with Maehata's physical fitness.

Women's Issues in Ballads By Baling

"The small drum is round and round, my mother beats me, how pitiful. I am my mother's floating heart grass, staying at home for a few years. I sweep the ground for other people, I burn incense for other people's Buddha, I call other people's mother 'Mom'. Her mother asks her what she eats? She says: Cooked tofu in a pot, rice to eat."

"Cabbage leaves, covering the ground, my mother gave birth to me, not strong enough; I ate my mother's milk since I was a child, and when I grow up, I serve other people's mother; other people eat rice, I eat bran, other people eat noodles, I drink soup; I'm so thirsty and miserable, I run to the backyard and cry a scene. The whip hits my body, I jump off a cliff, the cliff is deep: I jump into a well, the well water is small: I cling to the well bridge and take a look, I see the willow tips of my mother's house, willow tips, magpies are calling, who knows my grievance?"

The above two ballads are very popular in northern China. After reading them, we deeply feel how pitiful a miserable woman is who unfortunately becomes someone else's maid.

Indeed, we are all the same kind of human beings, why is it that on the one hand, one can enjoy as much as possible and not think it is strange? On the other hand, one has to bow down and serve, and be subjected to extreme abuse and oppression everywhere? This is human inequality, and it is indeed a distorted state in current society.

"Rescue the maids, ban the custody of maids." These two slogans have been chanted by the leaders of the women's world and those who care about women's issues in the past. Moreover, the government has also issued orders, but in fact, tens of thousands of maids have not been rescued and liberated. What a pitiful and urgent thing to rescue!

"Save the maids and free them from the sea of ​​suffering as soon as possible!" This is the cry revealed in their own ballads, and it is also a problem that the women's world cannot ignore.

Mother's Love By Yan Chonglou

The child's eyes do not yet contain the mother, but the mother's love already contains the child.

The mother has long held a passionate love for her child. When the child is still gestating, the mother has had many beautiful dreams for the child. She dreams of the child's bright eyes, apple-colored cheeks, lotus root-like limbs... The child in her dream is so lively and lovely! Although the mother often suffers from mental trance and physical discomfort for the sake of the child.

On the one hand, the mother hopes that her child will be born sooner, on the other hand, she hopes that her child will not be as stupid as the children she has seen before, so as not to betray her expectations; finally, on a stormy night, the mother's abdomen cramps, the mother's fresh blood flows, and the child falls to the ground with a cry.

In the child's ignorant cry, a smile appears on the mother's face. She wants to put the child beside her, watching the child from time to time. She is like a painter who has completed his masterpiece, only appreciating his masterpiece with satisfaction, and forgetting the hard work he spent in painting the masterpiece.

However, the mother's hard work has not yet ended. She must feed the child with milk at all times, and she must always consider the child's cold and warmth; sometimes when the child is sick, she becomes even more upset and loses her appetite and sleep! She must wait until the child's illness is cured before her heart can be at peace.

As the child gradually grows up, the mother's expectations for the child also increase with age, because the mother's love for the child is also accumulated deeper and deeper; if the child is weak and incompetent, then the mother's efforts will be in vain. Wouldn't she fall into the abyss of despair!

Although the child is now gradually growing up, his development is not yet sound, and his wisdom is not yet sufficient. In addition to the mother's love, the bad environment may also be in danger of corrupting him.

So how should the child strive for his own future? How should he cherish his life? How should he repay his mother's love... All of these depend on the child's heart, and wait for the child to answer with facts in the future.

Another Column: Epitaph for Zheng's Mother, Madam Hong By Chen Baozhen

Yongchun's Zheng Yushe formerly served in my ministry. This autumn, he came to Beijing to visit, presented the biography of Madam Hong, and requested an epitaph, tearfully saying: Yu Shu was born five years before my mother passed away. At that time, my late father was still traveling. Yu Shu and his younger brothers Yu Lin and Xiang Lin were young. The ceremony of decorating the end was mostly incomplete. After my late father's death, my mother's life was recorded in the epitaph written by Mr. Wu Zengqi, but my mother's family was not detailed. My mother has no extraordinary deeds. What Yu Shu knows and can describe are all ordinary things within the family. If I can obtain your words, describing what Mr. Wu did not mention, so that the Zheng family can follow it as a model for women for generations, then my mother will not die. According to the biography, the Madam was from the Hong family of Nan'an, the granddaughter of the Grand Master Jiang Huai, who was granted the title of Grand Master of Central Administration, and the daughter of Zheng Zhijing, a member of the local gentry. At the age of ten, she married Zheng Jun Yuanru. At that time, Grand Master Jiang Huai was a commercial magnate in the county, known as a rich man. The Madam grew up in a prestigious family and was physically weak and prone to illness. Her parents-in-law treated her with consideration and did not allow her to do hard work. The Madam said: A woman has a duty, how dare I shirk it. In addition to serving her parents-in-law every morning and evening, she personally handled everything from large events such as sacrifices and banquets to small tasks such as cooking and washing. Her father-in-law once suffered from a carbuncle on his neck, and she applied medicine twice a day and provided nourishing tonics before dawn for six months without fail. At that time, her parents passed away in succession, so she took in her younger brothers and sisters and raised them with care. People said that it was rare to see a married daughter be so attentive to her father's family, which showed the sincerity of her nature. She got up early to supervise her children's studies and prepared meals for the tutors at night, often doing it herself. When there were wind and rain, she would share food with the attached scholars. Her family affairs were already busy, but relatives often asked her to help with needlework, and she could not bear to refuse. She treated herself very frugally; because she was sick, her relatives gave her ginseng from overseas, but she would always share it with her family. Her silk and brocade were plentiful, but she often wore mended clothes. She worked hard and rested little, and she often suffered from dizziness. When it occurred, she would lie in bed and refuse to eat or drink, but after a short while, she would force herself to get up and take care of things as usual, which showed the decisiveness of her conduct. In the Guangxu year of Xin Chou, her uncle, Wei Ting, passed away without illness. The brothers of Yuanru were not home as guests, and his sister-in-law was in labor, so she took on all the internal and external affairs. In the end, she fell ill from overwork, and then cried for her deceased daughter, which made her even more unable to support herself. Initially, the Grand Madam had arranged for Yu Shu to marry a daughter of the Hong family. At this time, knowing that she would not recover, she held Yu Shu's hand and said to him: Since I became a member of your family for more than ten years, I have been fortunate enough to avoid mistakes. Now your generation has not yet been established, and my daughter-in-law will not see me, it is the will of Heaven! She cried out. Not long after, she passed away, at the age of only thirty-five. Yu Shu also said that more than two years after his mother passed away, Yu Shu married and became a student of the local school. More than a year later, he had a son. When he entered the officialdom, he welcomed his father to the post and missed his mother's hard work even more, so he had a pavilion built next to the tomb and named it "Thinking of Mother," but the wishes of both mother and son are all deeply sad. I believe that a person's son has a heart that cannot bear to let his parents die, so filial piety and love will last forever, so what space is there between the living and the dead? Now, although the Madam did not enjoy a long life, her descendants are prosperous, and her reward is in her afterlife. Heaven's praise of virtue is not false. I use this to comply with Zheng Sheng's request and write it on the tomb, so that those who cultivate feminine virtue will not doubt the principle of good fortune. In the month of Zhongqiu of the year of Zhangdun Zang, Chen Baozhen of Min County wrote it.

Xi Ge By Xueying

Whenever I walk to a place with bamboo, I often think of the large bamboo garden at my sixth aunt's house and the many unique square bamboos planted on the flower stand in her courtyard. Indeed, bamboo seems to be a specialty or a trademark in their family. Whenever people talk about Sixth Aunt or anyone in her family, I would immediately think of bamboo. At that time, I was still young, so of course I didn't know how to appreciate the charm of bamboo and the integrity it represents. I only felt that going to their house in the hot summer seemed cooler than other places, but going there in autumn or winter seemed particularly desolate. I didn't know anything else.

In a study surrounded by bamboo, there were often only two people lingering there. One was my uncle—the son of Sixth Aunt—and the other was Xi Ge, his son. Xi Ge was a very stubborn young man with great courage. He often stayed alone in that old study, which was two or three hundred steps away from the main house; but he didn't like to study. He liked gymnastics and sports very much. His personality was close to the martial arts side, so he was not loved by his uncle, who regarded himself as a "family of scholars," even though he was an only son. Later, probably because his personality was too stubborn, his uncle couldn't resist him, so he let him enter the military academy, and after graduating, he immediately officially enlisted in the army. Because he had enlisted in the army, I remember that every time a civil war broke out or a bandit suppression mobilization was held, his uncle and aunt were most worried. They would send someone to buy newspapers early every day, busy trying to find out if the 62nd Division to which Xi Ge belonged had participated. Fortunately, Xi Ge served as a soldier for five years, starting as a platoon leader and rising to the rank of battalion commander. In terms of seniority, he was also a lieutenant colonel. He probably returned to his hometown once every year, and each time his uniform seemed more spirited than the last, but his stubborn personality remained unchanged.

This summer, I suddenly received a message that Xi Ge was dead. How did he die? Was he killed in battle? No, he committed suicide. At that time, I was very shocked, so I inquired carefully from all sides, and finally learned the details of the matter.

It turned out that his troops were ordered to move to a small coastal county in the spring. This was a place where warships of a certain country often appeared. Many soldiers on the ships openly went ashore to take pictures or draw maps. The previous garrison often dealt with them with an attitude of trying to avoid trouble, so nothing happened. When Xi Ge arrived there, the same thing happened again after a few months. How could he tolerate it? He immediately ordered his troops to capture several soldiers from a certain country and also destroyed their cameras and the maps they had drawn. Then he released them. Unexpectedly, the next morning, soldiers from a certain country brought a number of small sampans, and fifty or sixty of them landed, also carrying ample weapons. They were obviously looking for trouble. Xi Ge was not afraid at all, and lined up his troops to wait in formation outside the city, which scared them back. Xi Ge thought that the matter must have come to an end, but who knew that half a month later, another battalion of officers and soldiers suddenly came to take over the defense. Because Xi Ge was surprised by their sudden arrival, he asked the new battalion commander; this person honestly told him that because of the protest of a certain country, their division commander had taken the blame, and his immediate superior—Commander Dong—had taken the responsibility for this matter himself because of his teacher-student relationship with him, and quietly resigned. Now, as long as he is transferred, there will be no problem. Xi Ge was extremely indignant after hearing this, and immediately shot himself in the camp headquarters. None of his subordinates knew that he was not crying: and this heroic and promising young military officer lightly sacrificed himself under his own stubborn personality.

The bamboo, with its straightness and joints, symbolizes him.

This Newspaper's Special Feature: Ms. Yang Jinxun Talks About Aviation Life By Ping

Learning Elementary Flight

One Must Seek Further Education

To Repay the Motherland

Women Learning Aviation

More Suitable Than the Army and Navy

I Hope Everyone Will Work Hard

"The drums are thumping, drumming up the courage of our soldiers. One drum thunders, the second drum mountains roar, and the third drum waves surge!..." This is the most magnificent section of the military song I sang in the Boy Scout troop when I was young. It is deeply imprinted in my mind and will never be erased; now that the national crisis is becoming more urgent and the bandits and puppets are invading Suiyuan again, thinking of the scenes at the front, I hum this old tune involuntarily. Indeed, when the healthy sons and daughters of China mention national affairs, who does not feel their blood surging and want to do something loyal and brave to save the country? Men are like this, and women are no exception! The day before yesterday, I visited Miss Yang Jinxun and talked about many things, which were very practical and pertinent, and could serve as a wake-up call for modern women! She is a member of the China Flying Society and has long placed her aspirations in the aviation industry. After six months of training, she can already fly alone, which is certainly no easy task. The following is our dialogue:

According to my observation, Ms. Yang is young, but she is quite experienced in her words and deeds. Her attitude is sincere and dignified, and her will is strong and calm. At first, she was unwilling to express any opinions. She said, "I feel very small and my knowledge is very superficial, so I am not qualified to speak publicly." I said, "Don't be too modest. Coming from thousands of miles away like you, learning aviation and sacrificing all enjoyment is truly rare among modern women. Even if you don't brag about yourself, you should win glory for women." After repeated explanations, she finally allowed me to briefly describe her personal wishes.

First, she introduced her background: "I am originally from Changsha, Hunan. I am twenty-five years old this year. My parents are both healthy, and I have two younger brothers and two younger sisters. My family all lives in Wuchang. In the winter of 1929, I graduated from the Normal Department of Hunan Provincial No. 2 Middle School. In the past seven years, in order to make a living, I have wandered to many places, but unemployment and poverty have accompanied me most of the time. But these experiences have been of great help and benefit to me. At the same time, it has given me a lot of life experience and knowledge. To temper oneself in a difficult life is something that school education cannot provide. In the past, I have worked as a tutor, civil servant, typist, and library administrator, etc. These jobs were for life, not my own aspirations; my lifelong aspiration is still in aviation.

"When did you have the motivation to learn aviation?" "I have a great interest in aviation. Ever since I saw an airplane, I wanted to learn to fly. In the past, I just wanted to fly, but now I understand why I want to fly. I remember the 'January 28th' Songhu War. That year, I had just left Shanghai and was living in Peiping. Although I did not personally experience that war, I had the same tense heartstrings. Every day, I read the Shen Bao, and I only felt more depressed. The bombs in my heart were really about to explode! The enemy's planes came to our country at will to drop bombs, while our compatriots used their blood and flesh to fight. Tens of millions of people's heads and bodies were turned into meat sauce under the bombs, and they even didn't know where to go. Not to mention buildings. These impressions left us not with sadness, but with anger! What will happen if we gather everyone's anger and explode it? That is something that cannot be easily imagined, but this thing that cannot be easily imagined will one day show its true face. Therefore, I prepared myself and decided to learn to fly, as the only goal in my technical training!"

Sketch—Ms. Yang

"How is your interest after joining the Flying Society?"

"There are only two female members in our society who are learning to fly, me and Miss Chen, but I believe that there must be many women who want to learn. I hope that women can account for a considerable number in the second phase of enrollment. In other countries' flight training classes, women are enthusiastically participating, and women also have various new records in the history of aviation. Can't the Chinese women's world produce aviation talents? We are naturally unwilling to lag behind. Taking advantage of the current government's promotion of aviation and the people's support, I hope everyone will work hard! In another month or so, we will graduate. This is only learning elementary flight. To serve the air force, we need more rigorous training. According to my experience in the past six months, I deeply feel that flying is not an extremely difficult thing. As long as you cultivate an indestructible body, have a fighting spirit

*The Shanghai News*, This City Supplement, *Ling Shu Jing* and *Su Wen*, Dr. Liu Xinbai, Main Answers, Red, Swollen, Toxic Conditions, No. 98, Mr. Yi Dongfan from the Third District Section of the Zhejiang Yuyao Andong City Liangzhe Salt Affairs Tax Police asks: The enemy has a sore, not quite a sore, not quite a boil, three inches above and slightly to the side of the back of the left knee, which is difficult for Western doctors to diagnose. Then, use a large piece of flannel, spread a one-third inch thick layer of "Sanfloid" on it, heat it slightly over a fire and apply it. Change it once a day. (5) See (4).

單睪丸與疝氣

Single Testicle and Hernia 143

No. 100, Mr. Kang Bihang, No. 38, Yongheng Company, Ningbo Road, asks: I was born with only one testicle, located on the left side. It is commonly said that people with only one testicle, although it does not affect fertility, can only have either sons or daughters, not both. In the above condition, there is also a hernia on the right side, which caused severe pain yesterday. I discovered this condition when I was young, and it has been swelling year by year, and recently it has become as large as a peach, and I fear it will continue to grow. Please tell me (1) is it true that people with one testicle cannot have both sons and daughters? (2) Is there a cure? (3) What medicine should I take for the hernia to be effective? (4) Do I need to stay in the hospital for long-term treatment? (2) I will know after an examination. If it is a hidden testicle, surgery can cure it. (3) A hernia is a structural disease, and medicine is ineffective. (4) This disease also requires surgery. You need to stay in the hospital after surgery, but you do not need long-term treatment.

大量濃痰

Large Amounts of Thick Phlegm 144

No. 101, Mr. Deng Yong, No. 9, Lane 301, Rugao Road, Hongkou, asks: I previously wrote to you about my illness, and I am very grateful for your reply. Now I have several more questions. My condition is as follows: I have been diagnosed with bronchiectasis. I cough up three to four hundred cc of thick phlegm every day. I don't cough now, and I don't have tuberculosis. My spirits are generally good, and I don't have a fever. It's just the thick phlegm. I have to cough it up every day by noon, otherwise I feel very uncomfortable in my trachea, and I can even hear the sound of phlegm when I breathe. If I exert myself too much, then the phlegm feels a little more. But other than the phlegm, I have no other illnesses. What do I do every day? I take walks in the garden, but I don't do any exercise. I sleep from 1 p.m. to 3 p.m., and I take clear cod liver oil three times a day. I go to bed around 8 p.m. every night and get up around 6 a.m. Now I have several questions for you: (1) Will this condition often cause me to cough up blood? (2) What are the dangers if I cough up blood? (3) How can I prevent coughing up blood? (4) How should I treat it if I cough up blood? (5) Can I read, work, and exercise with this disease? (6) Is the work I am doing now suitable? (7) My development is still good now. I wonder if this disease can be cured in the future? (8) Is my stuffy nose related to my bronchiectasis? Answer: (1) No. (2) See (1). (3) Take "Sinocalcin" ten times a day, one tablet every hour. (4) See (1). (5) Light exercise is okay. (6) Suitable. (7) It can be cured naturally by gradually strengthening the body, but the effect is unpredictable. (8) Unrelated.

頻咳不已

Frequent Coughing 145

No. 102, Mr. Dun Difen, Shanghai Law School, Jiangwan Road, Zhabei, asks: My mother is forty years old and has had a cough for a long time, which occurs every autumn and winter. When it occurs, she coughs frequently and produces a lot of phlegm. Please explain (1) is it caused by physical weakness? (2) What medicine should I take? (3) Is it lung disease? Answer: (1) Elderly and frail people often develop coughs in the winter due to the cold wind. Similarly, people with this constitution are prone to acute bronchitis due to cold wind, which is another cause of coughing. (2) Take "Kresocal." (3) I will know after an examination.

And it is inappropriate for a scientist to introduce religion. (3) See (1) and avoid drinking tea, coffee, and alcohol.

(6) What medicine should I use to treat her? Answer: (1) Congenital syphilis. (2) Children with congenital syphilis often develop rashes on their bodies, such as small pustular rashes, eczema, roseola, smallpox, and papules. (3) The big one is iritis. (4) "Hutchinson's teeth." (5) The prognosis is poor if she is not treated. (6) Inject "606" and "Merson." The former is one injection per week (0.15), and the latter is one injection every three days. Please ask a doctor to decide the dosage.

談言從「人言可畏」說開去

Talking about "Fear of Human Words" 150

By Zinan

After Miss Ruan Lingyu was killed by the old moral code and yellow journalism, she left a suicide note saying "Fear of Human Words." In addition to making us feel sad and mourn the loss of a generation of artists, it also made us understand that yellow journalism can be used as a weapon to kill the weak.

However, when the remains of the weak are not yet displayed in the hall, yellow journalism is also called "public opinion." After the matter is over, it is still called "public opinion," until the second tragedy reappears, and the murdered person must be somewhat prestigious in society, attracting the attention of people in society. Otherwise, committing suicide quietly because of a piece of yellow journalism is equivalent to the death of a dog.

Naturally, the murdered person is a weak person. Otherwise, he would never obediently lower his head and submit to others.

Recently, the French Minister of the Interior, Sarraut, also committed suicide because he was slandered by right-wing newspapers.

Sarraut was a socialist and had written many political commentaries. In theory, he should not have committed suicide. Although his political opponents' newspapers slandered him by saying that he "deserted during the European War," wasn't he "proven innocent" after investigation? Since he has been proven innocent, from the opposite point of view, it fully exposes the other party's shameless slander, and he has suffered no loss to his personality and reputation.

However, Sarraut finally committed suicide. This cannot but make us call him a weakling.

A socialist, a warrior, should show his courage even more when attacked by the enemy. This battle is not only for himself, but also for the masses. Fortunately, Sarraut's suicide occurred after the truth was revealed. Otherwise, wouldn't it give the enemy a better excuse for "suicide out of fear of punishment"?

If it is said that his suicide was for family matters, because his wife passed away eighteen months ago, his old mother's health was weakened after surgery recently, coupled with this decisive slander, he "felt that life was meaningless." The situation is true, and a person of flesh and blood always has his emotions, but is suicide a solution to the problem? What's more, a warrior only has the qualifications to kill and be killed, and has no right to commit suicide.

However, Sarraut committed suicide. In this regard, he showed his weakness and lost the heroic spirit of a warrior.

Speaking of killing, it is naturally inevitable in national disputes, but it must be done with a clear attitude. If you play tricks, fabricate rumors, and rely on cold arrows to hurt people and win victory, then even if you rely on cold arrows and slander to make the other party fall, victory is still slim. The reason is very clear. Cold arrows can only be hidden in dark corners, shooting a few arrows secretly. To openly charge into battle, you can't use it. And the decision of victory can only be seen in the melee of charging into battle.

Cold arrows can naturally shoot down a few people sometimes, but most of those who are shot are weak. After being shot by an arrow, they will fall to the ground and be unable to get up again. Even if they only hurt some skin, after the injury heals, they will always think that they have become disabled. The strong are different. Even if they are hit by a dark arrow, they will heal their wounds and fight again, and the cold arrow will increase his anger, and he will fight even more desperately.

The difference between the weak and the strong is probably in these places.

「賽金花」觀感

Thoughts on "Sai Jinhua" 151

By Mosi

I am glad to see "Sai Jinhua" being staged.

Although the subject matter of "Sai Jinhua" is a fact from thirty-six years ago, because this fact is almost the same as the current situation with foreign enemies invading and traitors selling the country, we do not feel that this is a historical drama, but rather a drama about our generation. Naturally, after seeing the ugly state of high-ranking officials bowing down to foreigners, we cannot ignore the playwright's enlightenment to us about Sai Jinhua: "It is useless to save the country for the traitors!"

A script with such national defense significance is very necessary to stage at the moment when the national crisis has reached the point of life and death.

Regarding the production of "Sai Jinhua," I feel that the playwright has "cinematized" it. It is so, unfolding scene by scene. If it were on the screen, it would indeed provide the director with easy and concise assistance. But, on the stage it is different. The more scenes there are, the more the scenery etc.

Page 20

cost. And the separation of time to change the scenery every time will cause the audience to interrupt their spirit during the performance. I don't think it is a good way to divide the number of acts too much.

In fact, the third scene can be omitted. The drama before this scene originally only exposed the violence of the Allied forces. But this point can be explained in a few lines of dialogue in the fourth scene.

The performance has not changed much from the original work. It's just that the first part of the movie is missing. Lantern slides were used to show subtitles such as "1900 (the 26th year of Guangxu, Gengzi) in Beijing" as "a comic illustration in a tragic era," with the sound of cannons and yellow smoke being set off in front of the curtain. The curtain fell. Although this is not as good as the original, it is better than nothing.

Regarding the entire performance, I think what they worked hardest on was the costumes, scenery, and props. It is indeed not easy to be able to do this.

Perhaps it was because the time to prepare for the performance was too rushed! Every actor's lines were not memorized well. If the lines are too raw, it will cause the dialogue to lack emotion and hinder the acting, and it will affect the tempo of the tune.

Because of the raw lines, the things on the stage seemed to lack emotion. Yes, some dialogues can also elicit laughter from the audience, but this is the success of the lines themselves. Such as: "The emperor only allows us to study. We can't do anything else besides studying." "The slave only knows how to kowtow, to kowtow to the foreigners!"

王瑩師賽金花

Wang Ying as Sai Jinhua 152

The most significant impact of this shortcoming on the script is in the fifth scene. The negotiations between Li Hongzhang and Waldersee are very important, but they do not show a sense of tension.

The director handled the seventh scene the best. The stage of that scene has a northern flavor. For example, Sun San came on stage to report that Sai Erye could not be rescued. Sun San took the package to leave, and we saw the competition between him and Gu Ma through the crack in the door curtain. Sun San escaped, heard the horse chirping, and then said that even Sai Erye's iron leather Qing was taken away. Sai Jinhua first called Gu Ma outside the door before coming on stage. These are all very good. The relatively poor one is the third scene, which is too hasty, making the audience unable to grasp any impression.

The actors do have many commendable things in their acting skills. However, restricted by the fact that they did not memorize their lines well, they could not develop to the fullest extent. Wang Ying's Sai Jinhua was quite good in the seventh scene. Unfortunately, she was overshadowed by Xia Xia's lively movements and vivid lines. In the fourth scene, Sai Jinhua was not enthusiastic enough when she met Waldersee, and she seemed too cold to attract Waldersee. I always feel that Wang Ying's actions cannot express the alertness of Sai Jinhua's character. Jinshan's Li Hongzhang is not bad in terms of acting skills. But his aura is not enough. The director gave him the best position in the fifth act, and he tried his best to perform, but he was too showy. Mei Xi was very good in the first scene. As for the others, those who went from the screen to the stage, Wang Xianzai's lines were not natural enough, Zhang Yi's body was good enough, but his voice was not loud enough, and Sun Min's acting was appropriate.

The makeup is very successful.

However, the lighting is too bad. The top lights are not bright enough, there are no footlights, the sidelights are too weak, and they are shaking. The two Sport Lights upstairs are sometimes bright and sometimes dark, moving east and west. I don't know why?

Stage management also lacks organization.

Overall, this performance feels like the fruit of mature art.

螃蟹

Crabs 153

By Luo Yu

"What was the reason for smashing the house? Would people like you do it?" I asked him, walking behind him on the narrow embankment. He seemed very touched, turned his head, and raised his eyebrows very high.

"You may not believe it, yes, it wasn't like usual. Our family went as one person, as if we had mustered up the courage and were not afraid of anything." He looked again at the embankment in front of him and below, and then said: "Yang Jingtai has a tile house - you can't find such a grand tile house in Tianjin. The chimney is decorated with a bell, like a small pavilion. The yard has a carved wooden corridor and a paved path of square bricks. The houses are even taller than the buildings, but now it has become broken bricks."

He noticed the energetic fish jumping in the slanting sun in the fishing port. He went on to say:

"People rushed into the cellar. The women in the house were crying and trying to stop them. They also begged, but begging was useless. People pulled out many leather clothes, dazzlingly luxurious. This made us all think of our own rags, so we simply tore them into pieces. People also found thick account books. This is right, it is something smeared with the blood of fishermen, and it was also torn to pieces by the angry people. Everyone wanted revenge, wanting to smash this upstart who monopolized the fish tax to death."

After he finished speaking, he did not look back and continued walking forward. We were all thinking about related things.

I watched the clumps of white foam being swept to my feet by the small waves, and several seagulls flying in the evening breeze, beautifully calling to each other. The long embankment was like a plump T-shape, extending straight to the river surface, where there was a dense forest of masts, mixed with cooking smoke. I looked at him—my cousin's broad shoulders, the large hands carrying the basket, which were very strong. I also saw his lowered head, knowing the impact in his heart: that was probably saying: "Cousin, you still have money." Thinking of this, I felt that this contemplation was not good. So I asked about the tax donation.

He talked about the tax donation with a new kind of expectation. He said that new taxes were added every year, and it had already exceeded one hundred yuan. If the fish scale was established, everyone would not be able to survive. He also said that a boat cannot catch many fish; even if a good net is caught, it will go to Yingkou to pay off the debt. He also said that if the boat is not repaired, it will often have problems. Even people's lives are afraid to think about it: I listened to these, and fell into my grandmother's story, where the boat fell on its side, traveling like a flying fish, the giant wind slapping the golden stars, which was a terrifying and bleak night scene.

The boats on the river had all entered the port. The masts and sails were crowded together on both banks. The dense hulls of the boats were deep brown, and although old, they were full of the deep flavor of fairy tales. On the other side of the wide river mouth, a row of white sails was floating. We sat on the embankment opposite the river, waiting for the white sails and masts.

My cousin rolled up his trouser legs and took off his shoes. His large body and legs appeared particularly tall and long. His cheeks were thin and strong. His eyes had a super-cold calmness, watching the white sail very patiently, which was flashing sunlight towards the evening sun.

"Hey! Are there any big shrimps? "The loud voice reverberated in the evening air, and it took a long time to hear the echo: "No, there are no big shrimps: there are a few crabs."

"Look at the iron boat of the ×× devils, who specialize in buying big shrimps and also go to the river mouth to cast nets."

So he jumped into the mud, carrying the basket and stepping over. The boat had already dropped anchor. I saw him climbing onto the side of the boat with both hands, stirring his feet in the river a few times, and climbing up.

Several children were arguing loudly about buying new fish and shrimps.

After a while, he ran back, carrying a few crabs. The ghostly green crabs were poking each other with their carapace tips, and the long claws were climbing vigorously, spitting foam as if intoxicated when they heard the sound of the port water.

An hour later, I sat in the courtyard with my aunt's family and ate boiled crabs. The south wind in September brought the sea breeze, and I felt a different realm that I had not thought of and was troubled by.

憂鬱

Melancholy 154

By Luzhi

It's like I walked into a spring forest, full of bird sounds in my ears, full of colors in front of my eyes, but I am more melancholy. More melancholy, because what I hear is a melancholy sigh, what I see are melancholy and hungry eyes, when I carefully examine my surroundings.

How far away is spring from us? No, our hopes are not that extravagant. We want only pleasant sounds, pleasing colors. All we want is a moment of rest, even if it's just a moment, allow us to escape from the encirclement of melancholy, lie down quietly, lick the wounds given by life, and caress the bleeding wounds. But although hope is low, as low as not having hope at all, we cannot achieve this low hope either. Is it foolish? If the reason for living in melancholy is foolishness, I will curse those clever humans - squeezing blood and juice from their fellow humans, or using sweet methods to snatch what they need from their fellow humans. If these behaviors are clever, then humans should not praise the words left by those philosophers, and should not use the words and deeds of those philosophers as a label. Ah! How foolish I am, this proves that my foolishness is a fact, the reason why humans praise and label those dead people is just like using a rein to control a wild horse to control another group of people who are considered foolish, simple and honest!

I have traveled through several provinces and encountered tens of thousands of people. Some of them I know well, and some I met hastily. I have seen the melancholy in their hearts. For the sake of life, for a little hope, they struggle, struggle, and finally let out that inherent long sigh, and then bury their heads and go back to life. I am always encountering these people living in melancholy.

Why do people always have this same face? I can't believe that I was born in a melancholy country, because I once wandered to an island nation called gentle and beautiful to prove that other countries would be better than my homeland, but it was the same there. The people there, the ones I could see, also had a long, melancholy face, a long, melancholy sigh. I can't help but think, so the world is full of melancholy everywhere, and people are born to be melancholy.

My certainty cannot but be overturned when I hear that there is indeed a land on earth that melancholy cannot extend to, a country that once lived in long-term melancholy and finally drove out melancholy. I find proof, even if it's a fact as small as a speck of dust flying from that land. Indeed, I cannot but revise my certainty: people are not born and grow up with melancholy, but the melancholy are caused by foolishness - but this foolishness is not the foolishness of every person, but the foolishness of the melancholy people. Why do they let those wasters, extravagants, and people who plunder the joy in their hands exist!

I have received enlightenment, received the greatest permission, I will go to the crowd full of melancholy sighs and melancholy eyes again, and say: We should not be melancholy, our melancholy is unreasonable!

Wang Shijie Arrives in Shanghai Today 169

(20th, Nanjing Dispatch) Minister of Education Wang Shijie departed for Shanghai at 11 PM on the 20th to attend the 30th anniversary celebration of Shanghai University. Lei Zhen accompanied him. It is reported that Wang also intends to inspect Shanghai Medical College and Jiaotong University on this trip, and is expected to return to Nanjing on the morning of the 23rd.

Shanghai University 30th Anniversary Today 170

Shanghai University, established six years before the founding of the Republic of China, has now reached its 30th anniversary. Through the efforts of successive presidents and the cooperation of faculty and staff, as well as the unity of teachers and friends, it has moved forward and developed year by year. The school's base has increased from over one hundred acres to more than four hundred acres, and over forty school buildings of various sizes have been constructed. Science halls, libraries, gymnasiums, sanatoriums, and other facilities are fully equipped. Statistics show that the entire school and its affiliated departments currently have over a thousand students. Yesterday (the 20th) was the first day of the school's 30th anniversary celebration. The campus decorations and lanterns were magnificent. A lantern parade was held at 7 PM, with over a thousand faculty, staff, and students participating, marching and cheering. Firecrackers were also set off, including beautifully arranged fireworks. Today, to celebrate the 30th anniversary, a review of military training students and Boy Scouts will be held at 8 AM. At 1 PM, there will be an alumni celebration banquet. At 3 PM, the 30th anniversary ceremony will be held in the auditorium. It is reported that Minister of Education Wang, Mayor Wu, and former President of the Judicial Yuan Dr. Wang Chonghui will all attend and deliver speeches. At 5 PM, a tea party will be held in the library to entertain guests. At 7 PM, there will be a variety show (school history performance) with simultaneous broadcasting. The affiliated primary and secondary schools will hold achievement exhibitions. There will also be exquisite commemorative publications and various special issues distributed to guests. Regarding transportation, China General Omnibus Company and the International Settlement Route 9 Bus have been connected for convenience.

Shanghai Zhuanqiao and Other Schools as Guidance Areas Designated by Jiangsu Department of Education 171

In order to promote elementary education, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education has decided to implement a district-based guidance system. It is learned that the department has now decided to organize twenty-six schools, including Shanghai County Zhuanqiao Zhenxin, Hua Jing, and Songjiang County Zhuanqiao, into the Jiangsu Province Third Normal District Elementary Education Guidance Area. It is reported that the guidance plan will be implemented in four phases over a period of two years.

Municipal People's Education Center Literacy Class Recent News 172

The central work of the Municipal People's Education Center this month is teaching phonetic symbols. Since the 18th of this month, the center's Director of Teaching, Wang Chunxi, has been teaching from 9 AM to 10 AM every day, and the director of the People's School, Yu Jian, has been lecturing from 1 PM to 2 PM, demonstrating the shape and sound of the symbols with hand-guided drawings in great detail. In the past few days, an unusually large number of people have come to the center to learn, and all those attending the lectures have been concentrated in the center's lecture hall. During the teaching sessions in the morning and afternoon, hundreds of people gather in silence and order. It is learned that in response to popular demand, the center is planning to establish a Mandarin phonetic symbol training class, and registration will begin in the coming days with formal lessons to follow.

Jiangsu Department of Education Sends Personnel to Inspect Provincial Schools 173

Report being compiled for review by the department. The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, having begun the 25th year, formulated inspection guidelines in order to understand the current state of education in various provincial schools. Inspectors, including Tang Daohai, were dispatched at the beginning of the month to inspect the schools for evaluation. It is now learned that Tang and others have completed the inspections and are currently compiling reports for Director Zhou's review.

Tian Bo Lie to Lecture in Nanjing and Shanghai 174

Kang Xuanyi Immediately Heads South to Prepare. Professor Tian Bo Lie of Cambridge University, President of the International Historical Society, and Professor Kang Xuanyi, former Standing Committee Member of the Shanghai University Education Association, arrived in Beijing from Japan the other day. They have been visiting various cultural institutions for days and have been invited to give public lectures at Tsinghua University, Peking University, and the National Library. According to Kang, he was recommended by the Shanghai University Education Association last year to go to Japan for inspection and, with Visiting Professor status, used the library facilities of Tokyo Imperial University to study international politics and diplomatic history. Now that Professor Tian Bo Lie's lecture schedule at universities in Beiping has been set, Kang Xuanyi plans to head south in the coming days to prepare everything for Tian Bo Lie and report on his inspection in Japan to various schools.

Xikang Representative Ma Zezhao's Impressions of Shanghai Education Gratitude for Educational Support for Xikang Students Hope for Nationwide Admission of Border Region Students 175

Ma Zezhao, the representative of the people of Xikang stationed in Nanjing, came to Shanghai this time to arrange the admission procedures for Xikang students. He met with Chen Heqin, Huang Jingwan, Shu Xincheng, Liu Zhanen, Zheng Xigu, Shen Tilan, He Qingru, Wu Xiaoyou, and others to arrange the placement of Xikang students and led them to visit various places. The results were extremely satisfactory. After returning to Nanjing, Ma expressed his deep impressions and published his views on Shanghai education as follows:

(1) All undertakings in the border regions need to be developed, and the most important of these is to communicate culture and improve the people's intelligence. This has been the belief adhered to for many years. However, if Xikang students studying in the interior serve in the interior after completing their studies instead of returning to Xikang to work, then the so-called work of communicating culture and improving the people's intelligence can only be partially completed, not fully completed. The gentlemen of Shanghai's cultural and educational circles not only pay special attention to education in the border regions but also earnestly encourage the Kang students admitted this time to return to Kang to serve after completing their studies. This insightful view has truly grasped the core of the border region education issue.

(2) There are a total of eight Xikang students who came to Nanjing this time, and four have been admitted in Shanghai, including one admitted to Botong Middle School, two admitted to Shanghai Middle School, and one admitted to Mullen Middle School. The others, either because of their young age or because of illness, remain in Nanjing and cannot go to Shanghai for the time being. When I first met with Mr. Chen Heqin, he took the time out of his busy schedule to lead the separate negotiations, and with the consent of the other gentlemen, this matter was completely completed in a short period of time. Their enthusiasm and speed of handling affairs are admirable.

(3) The visits to various schools lasted a long time, and all the students were full of vitality. At the same time, we were informed by the authorities of each school about the school's history, the purpose of establishing the school, and the methods of operation, all in great detail. They also said that they will continue to strive to become not only the best middle school in our country but also the best middle school in East Asia. What a vigorous spirit this is, and how great will the achievements be in the future?

Currently, there are only four Xikang students receiving this kind of good education. It is my responsibility to introduce more of them in the future, and I hope that the capable educational authorities in Shanghai will admit and train more of them so that Xikang students can continue to come to Shanghai to study and return to Kang to develop education in the border regions. I also hope that educational schools and authorities across the country will adopt the Shanghai method of admitting border region students so that there is no school in the country without border region youth. This is not only the fortune of one area but the fortune of the entire nation.

Hu Yuanmin Returns Home After Completing Studies 177

After graduating from the Management College of Jiaotong University, Mr. Hu Yuanmin interned at the Jinpu Railway for one year. In the summer of 1933, he went to England to study transportation and industrial management at the University of Manchester, gaining a deep understanding of financial management and organization. This summer, he obtained a Master of Science degree in Engineering. Mr. Hu felt that this was not enough, so he went to the Pennsylvania Railroad in the United States for practical training to learn and observe, and also took the opportunity to inspect the transportation industries of the United States and Japan. He returned to Shanghai on the Russian Empress on the 17th of this month.

The Shanghai University Alumni Team participating in the match will gather at the Dahua Restaurant downstairs on Sichuan Road before 10 AM today.
